The main points are: (1) Each province and city should establish one nursery. (2) Start seedling cultivation immediately. (3) Send personnel to inspect seedlings every year. Kong Xiangrong Inspects River Defenses in Henan and Hebei

To Inspect the Yellow River Estuary Soon

Kaifeng Correspondence: Kong Xiangrong, Standing Committee Member of the National Economic Commission's Water Conservancy Committee and Deputy Chairman of the Yellow River Water Conservancy Committee, was recently dispatched by the Economic Commission to Hebei, Shandong, and Henan provinces to inspect river defenses along the Yellow River. It is learned that at 9:00 AM on the 6th of this month, Kong, accompanied by his secretary, special commissioner, and the Norwegian chief engineer of the Yellow River Water Conservancy Commission, Anlisen, as well as personnel dispatched by the Henan River Affairs Bureau, departed from Kaifeng in three cars, crossed the river at Liuyuankou to Chenqiao, and traveled west along the river embankment in the afternoon, passing through Fengqiu territory. A section of the embankment was entirely sandy, and the wind blew sand, making construction extremely difficult. Then, they entered Wuzhi territory, traveled north along the east embankment of the Qin River. It was found that the Qin River originally originated from the Taihang Mountains in Shanxi, but this summer's severe drought has caused the entire river to dry up. That night, they stayed at the River Affairs Bureau in Wushe County. At 7:00 AM on the 7th, they turned into the east embankment of the Yellow River, which was diverted in the 22nd year, along the west embankment of the Qin River. Chen Ruzhen, Director of the Henan River Affairs Bureau, also accompanied them on this trip. Boulders were piled up along the embankment. According to Director Chen, these boulders were donated by the Pinghan Railway Bureau because the Railway Bureau recognized the importance of the project upstream of the Yellow River Railway Bridge and donated more than 10,000 cubic feet for flood prevention in advance, which was a benevolent act. This dangerous section of the river is mostly built with stone dams to block floods. From here, the north of the river has Qingyou, and the south has Guangwu Mountain, which can use natural forces to control the river. After the inspection, they returned to Wuzhi along the embankment. In the afternoon, they traveled south along the east embankment of the Qin River, visited the River God Temple, which was built with the remaining funds from river management that year, and then went to the north bank of the Yellow River Bridge, where they saw many stones thrown under the bridge piers, and the riverbed was heavily silted, only a few feet away from the tracks above the bridge. They then went east along the Rongze embankment, where the embankment surface was flat and planted with poplars and willows. After returning to the River Affairs Bureau, they also inspected various dangerous worksites in Zhengfan and Zhongmufan before returning to Bian via the Hei-gangkou Liuyuan dangerous work sites. By the time they arrived at the city wall, it was already 11:00 PM.

Furthermore, it is reported that Kong will discuss post-disaster projects on the Henan section of the Yellow River with Henan Chairman Liu Zhi and river affairs authorities on the 8th. After inspecting the joint Taigui Huayang embankment and Jiugulutidi embankment on the 9th, he plans to change to a large red boat and travel east along the river to Jinan to discuss river affairs with the Shandong provincial authorities, and plans to go to the mouth of the Yellow River to inspect the Sanwunkou drainage problem at the mouth of the sea. It is estimated that he can return to Bian on the 18th of this month.

Shandong Opens Small Mines on a Large Scale

Thirteen Sites Officially Underway, Slope Shaft Measurement also Started, Difficult Labor Compensation Still Yields No Results

Jinan Correspondence: The water robbery incident at the Rudak Mine has been going on for a month. Hundreds of workers are trapped in the water cave, and their bodies have not yet been recovered. The workers' families are crying to the heavens every day, which is the most tragic thing in the world. Regarding the issue of compensation, the company only agrees to give 302 yuan as compensation to each victim. The workers' families have repeatedly demanded more, but to no avail. Song Biru, Deputy Director of the Mining Affairs Office, and Director Zhang Shuheng went to Qingdao to ask the Rudak General Company for instructions. No telegram has yet arrived in Zibo. It is heard that Song and Zhang can return to Hongshan on the evening of the 9th. The Rudak Company will not stop opening small mines due to the opposition of the workers' families. On the 8th, all the small mines were started. In addition to the original six small mines in the North and South Shenmazhuang, four new small mines were opened in Chejiazhuang, and one small mine was added in each of the North and South Shenmazhuang, for a total of thirteen small mines. In addition, drainage engineering for inclined shafts is also underway. Kang Cun, the Measurement Director of Rudak, has been dispatched with staff members Li Dechun, Ten-Three, Wang Shizhen, and Sun Tanzhu to carry out the measurement. The location for the construction of the electric tramway has also been determined to be east of North Shenmazhuang, and a fourth layer of inclined shaft with a depth of 110 meters is being prepared to be opened, which will start soon. This project is contracted by Sun Changde and will take about four to five months at the earliest to complete. Currently, the water level in the Rudak mine is still rising rapidly, increasing by 17 millimeters per hour. It has now passed the third meter and a half of the fourth layer and is 107 and a half meters from the ground. Donations are still being remitted one after another. It is reported that Gao Qingtang, Standing Director of Rudak, has received 500 yuan, Ichikichi of Japan 1,000 yuan, Jin Yunpeng 1,000 yuan, and the Hua Wu Office 50 yuan, which will be distributed to the workers' families. (9th)

Jiangsu's 24th Year's Local General Budget Compiled, Deficit Supplemented by Financial Office

Zhenjiang News The general budget of Jiangsu Province for the 24th year has been compiled by the Financial Office for a long time. The deficit of 2.1 million yuan was decided by the Provincial Government Committee to be supplemented by the Financial Office. Now, it is learned that the Financial Office is trying to use the old land tax arrears over the years to make up for the shortfall. After this, the revenue and expenditure have been completely balanced, and the revenue and expenditure are 28,870,428 yuan. Under the heading of revenue, 1. Land tax is 11,910,000 yuan, 2. Deed tax is 1,192,000 yuan, 3. Business tax is 4,906,000 yuan, 4. Local property income is 346,607 yuan, 5. Local business income is 815,496 yuan, 6. Local administrative income is 400,001 yuan, 7. Judicial income is 512,424 yuan, 8. Subsidy income is 2,625,994 yuan, Debt income is 5.2 million yuan, 10. Other income is 961,907 yuan, totaling 28,870,428 yuan. Under the heading of expenditure, 1. Party affairs expenses are 203,760 yuan, 2. Administrative expenses are 2,634,351 yuan, 3. Judicial expenses are 2,802,366 yuan, 4. Public security expenses are 3,616,506 yuan, 5. Financial expenses are 1,200,160 yuan, 6. Education and culture expenses are 4,578,028 yuan, 7. Health expenses are 243,410 yuan, 8. Construction expenses are 7,982,678 yuan, 9. Local business capital is 54,000 yuan, 10. Assistance expenses are 692,074 yuan, 11. Pension expenses are 30,000 yuan, 12. Debt expenses are 4,390,082 yuan, 13. Reserve expenses are 294,013 yuan, totaling 28,870,428 yuan. The revenue and expenditure are completely balanced and formally established. Land tax accounts for the largest portion of the revenue, accounting for 41.25 percent, and business tax accounts for 16.99 percent, which is a significant increase compared to the past. Construction expenses account for the largest portion of the expenditure, accounting for 27.65 percent, followed by education and culture expenses, accounting for 15.86 percent.

Songjiang, Zhu Xing Robbery Victim Examines Injuries

Shen Yingu's home, a resident of Zhengliu Village, Zhujiaxing, Punan, was recently broken into by men speaking with a Qiyin accent, carrying guns and sticks. Shen Yingu, the victim, used to be a teacher and is currently bedridden due to illness. His son Xiancheng is a business partner, so the family is in decline. The thieves were misled by the rumor that the Shen family had property, so they tied up the father and son. Xiancheng's feet were injured. The clothes, fabrics, and ornaments in the house were all looted. Then, they went to the rooms of Shen Jinming, a member of the same clan, and Zhu Jicheng, a relative, to search. Although there was only a few dozen yuan in cash, the miscellaneous clothes, fabrics, jewelry, and beads used in each room were all taken away, worth about six or seven hundred yuan. When robbing Xiancheng's room, it was seen that one of the thieves was Jiangbei A-da, who used to run a twenty-one door gambling table in Zhujiaxing Town. After the incident, a list of losses was made and reported to the water and land police teams for investigation. The Zhu Shui police arrested Jiangbei A-da and sent him to the Zhujing Third Brigade for interrogation. Shen Xiancheng, who was injured, and Zhu Shenshi reported their injuries to the prosecutor's office of the court today.

Suzhou, Demolition of Enclosure Fields De-escalates

The dispute over the enclosure fields in Dongtai Lake has been reported in this newspaper. It is now learned that the county government dispatched personnel, together with the security team, leading 5,000 villagers, and started demolition on the 9th. As of the 11th, the dyke that cuts across Dongtai Lake and extends for fifteen li has been completely demolished, and the dike that is more than ten li long behind it has also been demolished. The demolition of the small dike in the new enclosure will begin on the 13th, and the demolition is expected to be completed in about a week. When the enclosure was demolished a few days ago, only about 50 guest villagers in the Nankuling Village area clashed with the villagers. At that time, the villagers Lu Azhang, Li Hulin, and Ye Zhilin were injured. Later, the security team Zhao came and dispersed the guest villagers. No other conflicts occurred in other places. County Magistrate Wu and Security Team Deputy Nie, who went to the countryside to command and suppress the villagers, have both returned to Suzhou.

Wuxi, Local Branch Court Ordered to Reorganize

Since the reorganization of the Wuxi County Court into a local branch court last year, in addition to this county, it has also accepted second-instance appeals of preliminary civil and criminal cases from Jiangyin, Yixing, and Liyang counties. Recently, the Ministry of Judicial Administration specially ordered the higher courts of various provinces to implement a three-level, three-trial system from July 1. Xu Tigan, President of the Wuxi Local Branch Court, has received instructions from the Jiangsu Higher Court, ordering him to start preparations immediately and reorganize on schedule. After the reorganization, it will only accept first-instance cases in this county and will no longer accept appeals. All second-instance appeals will be handled by the Jiangsu Higher Court. It is also heard that the Jiangsu Higher Branch Court will be established in Zhenjiang to accept second-instance appeals from counties north of the Yangtze River in Jiangsu Province, while second-instance appeals from counties south of the Yangtze River will be handled by the Jiangsu Higher Court, implementing a three-level, three-trial system.

Cotton Textile Industry Decides to Reduce Working Hours

Textile industrialists in Wuxi believe that due to the recent tense situation, tight credit, plummeting yarn prices, and complete lack of sales, yarn factories in places such as Tonghai and Jiangyin are suffering greatly and cannot maintain operations, and many have already implemented reduced working hours or temporarily suspended work. Wuxi is the most developed area for the inland textile industry. Although it has abundant resources, it is inevitably affected by the turbulent winds. Yesterday, the Cotton Textile Association convened a temporary meeting and discussed for a long time. Because the matter concerns the livelihood of laborers, it is necessary to consider both aspects. It was decided that each factory should independently consider the situation of its own factory and respond accordingly, according to the principle of reducing working hours by 30% to 50%.

Changzhou, School Representatives Demand Overdue Tuition Fees

The Education Bureau only raised and distributed one month of tuition fees for the schools in Wuyi for this semester. Schools in the city and countryside are struggling to survive in a very difficult situation. They are trying hard to support themselves, hoping that Education Bureau Director Qian Jinghu can raise and distribute one or two months before the Dragon Boat Festival to help them maintain operations. Unexpectedly, there was no news. The summer vacation is approaching, and everything must be concluded. There is no one to borrow from, and there is no solution. The schools have reached the end of their rope. The representatives of each school of the County School Joint Council had no choice but to go to the Education Bureau to ask Director Qian for instructions. Qian knew that he had no answer to this, so he expressed his resignation to thank his colleagues in the education field. On the 10th, he went to see County Magistrate Hou with the representatives of each school to explain the reasons for his resignation. County Magistrate Hou retained him at that time and promised to discuss it with the grain treasurer and try his best to find a way to ensure that the payment of education funds would be secured within one or two days. Then, schools in the city and countryside held a meeting to discuss that if the authorities still have no solution within these few days, they will convene an emergency general meeting to discuss the matter together.

Chongming, Two More Stores Closed

The stores in Chongming are also affected by the economic downturn. All industries are depressed. After the lunar Dragon Boat Festival, another foreign and general merchandise store closed. One is Liwanchang Foreign and General Merchandise Store in Beibao Town, which was opened in partnership for about five years. This spring, Dong Yushu started operating it alone. It suddenly closed on the 7th of this month. The other is Shunyu Xiang Foreign Goods Store in Jianhe Town, which opened in October last year with a capital of 3,000 yuan and was also established in partnership. Due to Wang Ruowu's mismanagement and sluggish business, it ceased operations on the 8th and announced liquidation.

Jingjiang, Farmers' Association Telegrams Support Jingjiang Daily

After the Jingjiang Daily was ordered to cease publication by Li Jinfang, acting magistrate of Jingjiang, and editor Liu Jianfan was convicted, Liu appealed to the Suzhou District Court. During the court hearing, Liu Jianfan requested the suspension of the detention and summoned Li Jinfang to court for questioning. Judge Zhu Qiao approved the supplementary summons and ruled to release Liu Jianfan on bail. The County Farmers' Association, representing the public, continued to appeal to higher authorities on behalf of the Chamber of Commerce and the Education Association for the newspaper to be published. The Qi telegram from the association is recorded below: To Yu, President of the Supervisory Yuan of the Central Party Department in Nanjing, Huang, Minister of the Interior, Chen, Chairman of the Provincial Party Department and Provincial Government in Zhenjiang, Yu, Director of the Department of Civil Affairs, Work-Supervisory Envoy of Jiangsu, Zhang, Fourth District Party Affairs Instructor of Nantong, Zheng Junjian, Administrative Supervisory Commissioner. The Jingjiang Daily in this county has been published for seven years. Its arguments are fair and the public regards it as their mouthpiece. Now, due to the publication of a novel, it has been ordered to cease publication by the county government. The public hopes that the newspaper will be republished and requests the association to appeal on their behalf. This association, as the representative of the public, follows public opinion and respectfully submits this telegram for review and approval, allowing the newspaper to be republished. We will await your orders. Wang Xulun, Director of the Jiangsu Province Jingjiang County Farmers' Association, kowtows respectfully.

Yangzhou, Chairman Chen and Others Visit Yangzhou for Inspection

Chen Guofu, Chairman of the Jiangsu Provincial Government, accompanied by Yu Jingtang, Director of the Department of Civil Affairs, Zhou Fohai, Director of the Department of Education, Ye Xiufeng, Standing Committee Member of the Provincial Opium Suppression Association, Hu Ding'an, Director of Academic Affairs of the Medical Administration College, and He Zhongxiao, Secretary of the Provincial Government, crossed the river by provincial government gasoline boat at 9:00 AM on the 10th, changed to a Zhenjiang-Yangzhou long-distance bus, and arrived in Yangzhou at 10:30 AM. Amidst military music, they got off the bus one after another, nodded in response to the welcoming people, and then walked across the river to the Chaoguan Life School. Chen Chaoxiu, the principal, led them into the design room. After a short rest, Principal Chen reported on the school's preparations for construction, enrollment, and establishment. Then, they went to observe each department. Finally, they took a photo with the teachers and students. At 11:30 AM, they left the school and went to the high school department of the Provincial Yangzhou Middle School. After arriving at the school, Principal Zhou Houzhu led them to inspect the female elementary life class. At noon, they had lunch in the dormitories of the class, which were organized into families. The dishes were all cooked by the students themselves and were very tasty. Before leaving, they passed the first kindergarten classroom affiliated with the provincial experimental elementary school. Just as the "Quiet Rest" class was being taught, Chairman Chen stopped to watch the innocent and lovely children, half asleep and half awake, and expressed his pleasure. When passing the school's newly built gymnasium, he entered and inspected it for a week, and then left the school at 2:00 PM and went straight to the Opium Addiction Treatment Center in Quekou Street to inspect it. He asked about the number of addicts in the center and the methods of detoxification. Chairman Chen personally visited the addicts' bedrooms, asking and persuading them. After leaving the center, he returned to the province at 3:00 PM.

Nantong: Opium Addict Factory to be Established by Month's End

The Jiangsu Provincial Anti-Opium Committee is trialing an opium addict factory in Xiaohai Town, Nantong. Yan Yinan has been appointed as the director. The project is progressing actively according to the predetermined plan and is scheduled to be completed by the end of the month. The Fourth District Security Command has already ordered the counties under its jurisdiction to send opium addicts to the factory to learn skills.

Lawyer Sentenced to Imprisonment for Seduction and Adultery

Wu Guixin, the vice president of the Nantong Lawyers Association, seduced his niece, Li Xiangzhi, and lived with her, resulting in a child. After their relationship fell apart, Li Xiangzhi sued Wu Guixin in court for seduction and breach of trust. After the prosecutor filed a public prosecution, Wu and Li suddenly reached a settlement. The criminal court concluded the trial and declared Wu Guixin not guilty. The prosecutor, dissatisfied, appealed to the High Court. The High Court has now sentenced Wu Guixin to one year and six months of imprisonment.

Jiaxing: Two Kidnappers Executed by Firing Squad

Abao, the son of farmer Feng Yungui from Li Lin Village, Xinfeng Town, Jiaxing (currently thirteen years old), was kidnapped by bandits in September of last year. In October, the Shanghai Public Security Bureau's Detective Team captured two bandits, Wang Chengzhong and Qian Jintu, in Shanghai. They confessed to committing a kidnapping case in Jiaxing and that the victim was hidden in Yuantong Temple in Shiba Li Bridge. The detective team immediately took the bandits to Jiaxing and, together with Jiaxing Public Security Bureau officers, arrested five bandits: Zhao Daxing, Yuan Yigen, Zhang Yimin, Huang Youmei, and Ye Laosan. They also rescued the victim, Abao. After interrogation in Shanghai, the suspects were brought back to the Jiaxing Local Branch Court for trial. On May 15th, Zhao Daxing, Zhang Yimin, and Yuan Yigen were sentenced to death according to the Regulations for the Punishment of Bandits. Qian Jintu and Ye Laosan were each sentenced to sixteen years of imprisonment. Wang Chengzhong was sentenced in Shanghai, and Huang Youmei was acquitted. It is reported that the Songhu Garrison Command sent military police to Jiaxing on the 10th to bring Wang Chengzhong and Huang Youmei to Shanghai. The judgment of the Local Branch Court has been submitted to the Provincial Government for review through the High Court. The two convicted kidnappers, Zhao Daxing and Yuan Yigen, were executed. After receiving the order, the Branch Court dispatched Prosecutor Wang Bangyan, accompanied by land and water police, to the Third Prison at 8:00 AM on the 11th to retrieve the two convicts, Zhao and Yuan. After verifying their identities, they were taken to the western suburbs and executed by firing squad. The charges were announced to serve as a warning.

Hangzhou: Relief for Chun'an Tea Farmers Resolved

The Zhejiang Provincial Government, to provide relief to tea farmers in Chun'an, ordered the Zhejiang Local Chinese Farmers' Banks to jointly issue loans of 80,000 yuan. It also instructed the Bureau of Commerce and Administration to properly arrange relief measures. After convening a meeting with tea merchants and farmers' associations, each tea firm was encouraged to buy as much as possible, and the customs brokers were encouraged to sell to the tea farmers quickly to avoid losses. It is reported that the Jianggan branches have over 10,000 loads of tea in storage. Through the efforts of officials and merchants, over 7,000 loads have been sold, with just over 2,000 loads remaining, which are expected to be sold within a week. Some tea farmers in Chun'an have already received funds and returned home. Meanwhile, Huang Renwang, the Administrative Inspector of the district, has advised tea farmers not to continue transporting tea leaves to the province.

Incompetent Doctor Sued for Murder

Weng, the wife of Shen Shuiqing, who resides at No. 26, Qianshi Lane, Hangzhou, suffered from intestinal obstruction. She hired Yang Shida, a forensic doctor at Ren'ai Hospital, to perform an abdominal operation. Yang's negligence in the operation caused the incision to not be sutured properly, resulting in a rupture and leakage of urine and feces from the wound. Yang ignored the situation afterward. Shen then filed a lawsuit with the Hangzhou Local Court Prosecutor's Office, accusing him of professional malpractice resulting in bodily harm. Weng died on the night before last at 11:00 PM. Yesterday, the court was notified for an examination and a request was made for strict punishment.

Young Woman Murdered

A stylishly dressed young woman, approximately in her twenties, was found murdered at a secluded rural spot near Lu Liu Temple, Shi Jia Bridge, outside Genshan Gate, Hangzhou, at 1:00 PM on the 10th. She was shot to death in front of a tomb next to the temple. She was wearing a white silk cheongsam and was shot twice, with the bullets entering from behind. The manner of death was exceptionally gruesome. The Local Court has been notified and has dispatched a prosecutor to lead an inspection and to strictly apprehend and investigate the perpetrators. The cause of death is likely related to either adultery or revenge.

Local News

Problem of Money Exchange Transfer Resolved; Special Committee of Money Exchanges Agreed on Five Measures the Night Before Last; Xu Kan Summoned Silver and Money Exchange Representatives Yesterday to Discuss Three Measures

The Xinsheng News Agency reports that after the Special Committee of the Money Exchanges Association resolved five measures regarding remittance transfers and collateralized lending discounts, it notified all firms to comply yesterday morning. The Money Exchange Joint Reserve Bank has decided to join the bank note exchange of the Bankers Association as an exchanger. The Bankers Association held an emergency meeting yesterday and approved the first of the five measures of the Money Exchanges, which concentrates remittance transfers into the reserve bank. It notified all banks to comply and formed a subcommittee to study remittance transfers and other issues. Financial Vice Minister Xu Kan summoned financial leaders yesterday afternoon at 4:00 PM to decide on three solutions, increased the number of members on the Money Exchange Supervisory Committee, and approved the measures requested by the Money Exchanges. Details are as follows:

Meeting of the Special Committee of Money Exchanges

The Money Exchanges Association held a board meeting at 3:00 PM the day before yesterday and decided to establish a special committee. It then held a committee meeting at its Ningbo Road location at 10:00 PM that night. Attendees included Qin Runqing, Pei Yunqing, Yu Zhuting, Qian Yuansheng, Liu Wuqiao, Bo Songnian, Shao Yanshan, Xie Taofu, Xi Jiming, Li Shoushan, Qin Xiqing, Wang Huailian, Sheng Xiaoshan, Chen Shengwu, and others. Vice Minister of Finance Xu Kan attended and participated. In addition to agreeing on five measures (see Money Exchange Notice), it was also agreed that the Money Exchange Joint Reserve Bank would join the bank note exchange of the Joint Reserve Committee of the Bankers Association. The meeting adjourned at around 2:00 AM yesterday morning.

Notification of Compliance with Five Measures

The Money Exchange Association notified its member money shops yesterday morning, stating: "Dear colleagues, the Special Committee has resolved the following: (1) All foreign currency remittances from banks currently deposited in various shops must be transferred to the Money Reserve Bank simultaneously. Thereafter, shops will no longer receive foreign currency remittances from banks. (2) Shops requiring remittance funds must borrow from the Money Reserve Bank by pledging collateral. (3) The Money Reserve Bank requiring funds may borrow from the banking syndicate by pledging collateral. (4) Collateralized loans made to the Central, China, and Communications Banks using deed pledges must be registered with the Ministry of Finance Supervisory Committee on the 11th of this month only. There will be no extensions. New deed pledges must also be registered on this day. All valuations will be calculated at 90% of the Bureau of Public Works' estimated value. (5) Collateralized loans made to the Central, China, and Communications Banks using government bonds will be valued at 100% of this month's market price. New loans will also follow this method. If the market price falls by 4 yuan, the difference must be paid. We are specifically notifying members of these resolutions to ensure compliance."

Emergency Meeting of the Bankers Association

The Bankers Association held its 68th emergency executive committee meeting at its Hong Kong Road hall at 2:00 PM yesterday. Attendees included Chen Guangfu (represented by Yang Jemei), Chen Zheqing, Ye Fuxiao, Wang Zhihua, Wang Boyuan, Tang Shoumin, Hu Xiann, Qu Jigang, Xu Xinliu, Zhu Zikui, Zhang Zhuyu, Xu Boming, Wang Zihou, Hu Bijang, Bei Songsun, Xu Jiqing, Jing Runshi, Wu Yunzhai, and Li Fusun. Tang Shoumin chaired the meeting, and Secretary-General Lin Kanghou reported. Discussions began immediately. (1) Regarding the first of the five measures set by the Money Exchange Special Committee, which states that "all foreign currency remittances from banks currently deposited in various shops must be transferred to the Money Reserve Bank simultaneously, and shops will no longer receive foreign currency remittances from banks," it was resolved to approve it and notify all banks to comply. (2) Regarding the Joint Reserve Committee's request to form a subcommittee to thoroughly study remittance transfers and other issues, it was resolved to approve it and jointly study with the Joint Reserve Committee. The China, Communications, Shanghai, Zhejiang Xingye, Zhejiang Shiye, Zhongnan, Continental, Jin Cheng, and Salt Banks were nominated as committee members. The meeting adjourned at 3:40 PM.

Financial Vice Minister Convenes Financial Meeting

Vice Minister of Finance Xu Kan convened a meeting of financial leaders at the Central Bank's boardroom at 4:00 PM yesterday to discuss rescuing the Money Exchanges, stabilizing finance, and calming the market. Attendees included Central Bank Deputy Governor Chen Xing, Business Bureau Manager Xi Demao, Bank of China Chairman Song Ziwen, Shanghai Branch Manager Bei Songsun, Communications Bank General Manager Tang Shoumin, Business Bureau Manager Zhang Peishen, Shanghai Bank Assistant Manager Yang Jemei, Zhejiang Xingye Bank General Manager Xu Xin, Zhejiang Shiye Bank General Manager Li Fusun, Guohuo Bank General Manager Song Ziliang, Guohua Bank General Manager Qu Jigang, Continental Bank General Manager Ye Fuxiao, Salt Bank Manager Chen Zheqing, Jin Cheng Bank Manager Wu Yunzhai, Zhongnan Bank General Manager Hu Bijang, China Industrial Bank General Manager Hu Mengjia, Siming Bank General Manager Ye Zhuotang, and Money Exchange Association Chairman Qin Runqing. The meeting adjourned at 7:00 PM.

Decision on Three Solutions

According to reliable sources obtained by the Xinsheng News Agency reporter, the meeting resulted in three solutions: (1) Remittance transfers will be concentrated in the Money Exchange Reserve Bank, with the Money Reserve Bank collecting collateral from various shops to guarantee this remittance transfer. (2) The Money Reserve Bank can exchange these collateralized assets for 1935 financial bonds from the Money Exchange Supervisory Committee. (3) The Money Reserve Bank can use these bonds to borrow cash from the banking syndicate. With the decision of these two solutions, the problem of remittance transfer circulation is completely resolved. It is reported that the Ministry of Finance's resolute proposal of 25 million yuan in financial bonds to exchange for collateral from the Money Exchanges to guarantee bank loans, ensuring that all parties are protected from losses, is indeed the best policy.

Acceptance by Foreign Merchants and Compradors Association

The Foreign Merchants and Compradors Association held a special meeting at the Jardine Matheson Bank on the Bund at 3:00 PM yesterday and resolved to accept the first of the five measures of the Money Exchanges, which states that "all foreign currency remittances from banks currently deposited in various shops must be transferred to the Money Reserve Bank simultaneously, and shops will no longer receive foreign currency remittances from banks." A reply was sent to the Money Exchanges Association, and the meeting adjourned at around 4:00 PM.

Money Reserve Bank's Membership in Exchange Approved

After the Money Exchange Joint Reserve Bank decided to join the Bankers Association's Joint Reserve Committee's check clearing house as an exchanger, the Xinsheng News Agency reporter learned from relevant sources that the bank check clearing house has approved the Money Exchange Joint Reserve's membership. Manager Zhu Boquan of the check clearing house and Manager Qin Xiqing of the Money Exchange Reserve Bank began negotiating the procedures for joining yesterday. The check clearing house originally had 38 member banks, but after the Minghua Bank withdrew, it had 37. With the addition of the Money Exchange Reserve, it returns to 38. It is reported that it will take effect starting today.

Ministry of Finance Increases Members of Money Exchange Supervisory Committee

The members of the Money Exchange Supervisory Committee were originally Xu Kan, Du Yuesheng, Wang Xiaolai, Qin Runqing, and Gu Yigu. According to the Xinsheng News Agency reporter, the Ministry of Finance has added Hu Meian, Shi Jiu'ao, Wang Zisong, and Xu Baoqi as members. The committee held a meeting at the Money Exchange Joint Reserve Bank at 3:00 PM yesterday afternoon, with all members attending. It is reported that the committee has accepted the fourth of the five measures of the Money Exchanges, which states that "[c]ollateralized loans made to the Central, China, and Communications Banks using deed pledges must be registered with the Ministry of Finance Supervisory Committee on the 11th of this month only. There will be no extensions. New deed pledges must also be registered on this day. All valuations will be calculated at 90% of the Bureau of Public Works' estimated value" and the fifth measure, which states that "[c]ollateralized loans made to the Central, China, and Communications Banks using government bonds will be valued at 100% of this month's market price. New loans will also follow this method. If the market price falls by 4 yuan, the difference must be paid."

Hope for Reduction in Remittance Transfer Fee

The Xinsheng News Agency reporter learned from silver and money exchange sources yesterday that (1) "remittance transfer" refers to the loan currency of inter-industry accounting that must be collected in cash the next day, and (2) "remittance transfer fee" refers to foreign cash that must be paid in cash on the same day. Yesterday, the remittance transfer fee on the Money Exchange market was still at a peak of 7 jiao. Since the Ministry of Finance convened a financial meeting and decided on three solutions, those familiar with the matter observed that today's remittance transfer fee will definitely decrease.

Jiangnan Railway Company Loan Established

Collateralized by Company Bonds of 2 Million at an 80% Discount; Underwritten by China, Communications, and Shanghai Banks

The Shanghai-based Jiangnan Railway Co., Ltd. needs substantial funds to build roadbeds. A contract has been signed to borrow 1.6 million yuan from the China, Communications, and Shanghai Banks by collateralizing the company's issued bonds of 2 million yuan at an 80% discount. The Xinxin News Agency reporter has recorded the details as follows:

Underwritten by Three Banks

The Jiangnan Railway Company has a fixed capital of 6 million yuan. Apart from the 3 million yuan already paid in, it has now passed a resolution at the second shareholders' meeting on the 10th of this month to issue bonds of 3 million yuan to complete the Nanjing-Helixi section of the railway project. The bonds are divided into 3,000 shares, each with a face value of 1,000 yuan. The entire fixed assets listed in the company's balance sheet and property ledger as of the end of June 1935, totaling 6 million yuan, will serve as joint collateral for the bonds, giving it a strong credit rating. The China, Communications, and Shanghai Banks have agreed to underwrite the bonds, and subscriptions are very active.

Contract Signed

The company needs substantial funds to complete various projects. After discussions between General Manager Zhang Jingjiang and banking circles, it was decided to collateralize the company's bonds with a face value of 2 million yuan at an 80% discount to borrow 1.6 million yuan in cash from the China, Communications, and Shanghai Banks. The loan contract has been signed, totaling two copies: (1) China and Shanghai Banks jointly provide 1 million yuan with an annual interest rate of 1% and a term of 5 years; (2) Communications Bank provides 600,000 yuan with an annual interest rate of 1% and a term of 3 years. The above two contracts have been officially signed by General Manager Zhang Jingjiang of the company and the responsible persons of each bank. The funds will be disbursed as needed for the project.

Repayment in Installments

The repayment method for the loan has also been decided as follows: (1) 1 million yuan from China and Shanghai Banks will be repaid in installments over five years: 10% in the first year, 15% in the second year, and 25% each year for the third, fourth, and fifth years; (2) 600,000 yuan from Communications Bank will be repaid in installments over three years: 100,000 in the first year, 200,000 in the second year, and 300,000 in the third year. The repayment period will begin when the company starts operations. Interest will be paid annually.

Japanese Ambassador to Arrive in Shanghai This Afternoon; Proceeding to Beijing Tomorrow Morning to Present Credentials on the 14th

Japanese Ambassador to China, Akira Ariyoshi, returned to Japan last month to report on the situation in China and has now completed his mission. According to the Japanese Consulate-General in Shanghai, the Shanghai Maru, carrying Ambassador Ariyoshi, is scheduled to arrive in Shanghai at 2:30 PM this afternoon and berth at the Huishan Wharf. The Japanese Consul-General in Shanghai, Ishiya, the Consul-General in Beijing, Suma, and Japanese military generals stationed in Shanghai will be present to welcome him. Yu Ming, Director of the Shanghai Office of the Chinese Ministry of Foreign Affairs, and Wang Changchun, Commissioner of the Municipal Government, will also be present to welcome him. After a brief rest, the Japanese Ambassador will travel to Beijing by train tomorrow morning, accompanied by Counselor Arino and Secretary Yokokawa, to present his credentials to the Chairman of the Chinese Government at 11:00 AM on the 14th.

Gu Xinyi Discusses Gradually Reducing Purchases of Foreign Rice

Merchants Have No Reason to Want to Purchase Foreign Rice; Domestic Production Should Be Increased Year by Year

Although China claims to be an agricultural country, the number of foreign rice imports in recent years has been truly alarming. Both the government and the public are thinking of ways to remedy this. Chen Gongbo, Minister of Industry, plans to gradually reduce the purchase of foreign rice by rice merchants, limiting it to one-tenth each year. The Central News Agency reporter asked Gu Xinyi, a prominent figure in the food industry, about this matter. His response is as follows:

Domestic Production Should Be Increased

According to Gu, the sharp increase in foreign rice imports in recent years is due to the expansion of areas affected by natural disasters in China, which has greatly reduced harvests. It is necessary to purchase foreign rice to supplement the supply. This is certainly not what the Chinese people want. Now, the authorities should passively increase the tax on foreign rice and actively make farmers' lives more stable and improve production techniques. Then, domestic grain production will increase, and foreign rice can be eliminated. Therefore, as long as domestic rice production is sufficient to maintain the people's food supply, merchants will have no reason to purchase foreign rice again. If the purchase is to be reduced year by year, it should be done by increasing domestic production year by year.

No Siamese Rice Imports

The Central News Agency reporter asked Gu whether rice merchants could stop purchasing Siamese rice because the Siamese authorities are mistreating Chinese residents in Siam. Gu replied that although Siam is a rice-producing country, its rice is not suitable for sale in China. In fact, there are no Siamese rice imports.

Zhu Jingzhou Traveled to Beijing Last Night

Will Take Eurasia Plane Back to Gansu Today; All National Taxes in Gansu Have Been Returned to the Central Government

Zhu Jingzhou, Director of the Gansu Provincial Department of Finance, came to Shanghai from Beijing some time ago to negotiate a loan and has now completed his work. He took the night express train to Beijing last night and will transfer to the Eurasia plane back to Gansu. The reporter visited Zhu at his residence yesterday afternoon. Zhu had just recovered from a fever and his spirit had not fully recovered. The interview is recorded as follows: (Q) (Reporter's question) I recently heard that Gansu has returned all kinds of national tax revenues to the central government. What is the situation? (A) (Zhu's reply) Following Chairman Zhu's instructions, I have long wanted the central government to directly collect taxes that are national in nature to comply with government orders. In addition to the stamp tax, which has long been handled in accordance with the ministry's orders, we have now eliminated the special tobacco tax collected in Gansu from July 1, which has been approved by Director Kong of the Tax Bureau and formally notified to the Gansu Provincial Government. (Q) I heard that the salt tax has also been changed to be directly collected by the central government. Is that true? (A) The salt tax is not directly under the jurisdiction of the Department of Finance, so I don't know the details. However, Chairman Zhu did ask the Ministry of Finance to take over with the utmost sincerity. It is reported that Director Kong has already agreed. In short, all matters discussed between the Ministry of Finance and the Gansu Provincial Government this time were approached with the utmost sincerity, washing away the bad habits of haggling of former officials, which is indeed a good phenomenon between the central government and the local government. (Q) Is there a set date for returning to Gansu? (A) Because Chairman Zhu has repeatedly urged by telegram, the Eurasia plane has been scheduled to fly directly back to Gansu on the 12th. (Q) I heard that Chairman Zhu plans to invite leaders from Shanghai's financial and industrial circles to Gansu for inspection. Has this been decided yet? (A) Many people in Shanghai's financial circles are old acquaintances. I have been ordered to extend the invitation, and many are willing to go. However, due to the current financial turmoil, all circles feel uneasy, so the departure date may have to be postponed. (Q) What is the climate like in Gansu? (A) Based on my experience in the past two years, the climate in Gansu is truly warm in winter and cool in summer. Its good climate is unmatched in the country and is beyond what most people expect. People in China who have not been to Gansu often think that it is a cold and desolate place beyond the borders, which is very absurd.

Shanghai Banking Circles Believe Worldwide Adoption of the Gold Standard is Impossible

According to a Havas Washington dispatch, the International Chamber of Commerce Federation will discuss the adoption of the gold standard worldwide to achieve currency stability at its general meeting to be held in Paris on the 24th of this month. Yesterday morning, the Central News Agency reporter asked a banker in Shanghai about his opinion on this matter. He said that at a time when the world's finances are extremely panic-stricken, countries that have adopted the gold standard are abolishing it. Therefore, he believes that it is impossible to achieve currency stability by advocating the adoption of the gold standard worldwide. Moreover, the United States' silver policy is actively advancing, which puts this move in direct opposition to the United States. Furthermore, the financial policies adopted by other countries are mostly contrary to it, so this proposal may soon disappear.

Yangtze River Six Companies; Alliance Cooperates to Share Expenses for One Year

The sharing of water freight by the alliance of the Six Yangtze River Companies has been discussed by representatives of the six companies for more than half a year. The various measures have now been agreed upon and unanimously approved. The implementation period will be from July 1, with a trial period of one year (the previous report of half a year was incorrect) to June 30 next year. However, within this one year, the six companies may not withdraw from the alliance agreement without reason. Even by next year, if they do not want to continue, they must notify in advance three months before the expiration date so that a public decision can be made. If it is unanimously deemed beneficial, it can still be continued after the one-year term expires and the contract will be considered valid. With July 1 approaching, the representatives of the wheel companies convened another meeting yesterday afternoon to discuss the procedures to be handled after implementation.

Yesterday's City Party Headquarters Convenes Meeting with Teachers of Literacy Schools

Seeking to Finalize School Locations and Commence Enrollment; All Schools Officially Established Before the 20th

According to the Guomin News Agency, at 2 p.m. yesterday, the Literacy Education Promotion Association of the City Party Headquarters specially convened a meeting with teachers of literacy schools who had formally registered and been accepted by the headquarters. In attendance were the association's managing director, Tong Xingbai, and association staff members Mao Yun, Huang Tiren, Zhang Sheng, Gu Shaoyan, Wang Longzhang, Lu Yinchu, Yu Zhenhui, Peng Yongjie, and others, as well as 48 teachers. Tong Xingbai presided over the meeting, Huang Tiren served as recorder, and Lu Yinchu served as master of ceremonies. After the customary rituals, the chairman outlined the steps for promoting the literacy movement in the city and reported on the implementation methods and points that teachers should pay attention to when preparing. The details are recorded below:

Instructions: Roughly stated, today the City Party Headquarters has called everyone together for a discussion with a few intentions to share. This time, the city is organizing literacy education. This literacy movement is originally one of the seven movements. It has been done in the past, but because there was no collective effort, the results were poor. To handle this kind of major work, the joint effort of all groups in the city is necessary to achieve satisfactory results. This time, it is not only the Party and government that are organizing, but also all groups are united in doing so. The City Party Headquarters is the leader of all groups, so this Party Headquarters is leading 400 to 500 groups in the city to organize. With the power of 400 to 500 groups, we will definitely be able to completely eliminate illiteracy in the shortest possible time. However, many groups, due to location or talent constraints, have specifically entrusted us to handle it on their behalf. Groups are contributing financially. Currently, there are already 300 to 400 self-organized ones, and 50 to 60 that are being handled on behalf of others. However, the difficulty in organizing literacy education now, its success or failure, does not lie in the number of groups or the financial capacity. The key lies entirely in the talent and effort of the teachers. The first difficulty is recruiting students, because it is not easy for teachers to go and find students. The key is to make students always feel like they want to study and have the magic to arouse their interest in reading, which can be seen at graduation. Therefore, the teacher's responsibility is very important. If you only teach a thousand words or six hundred words, a primary school graduate is enough. Why is it necessary to have middle school or university graduates? The reason why we want to select strictly is that it is not just about teaching a few words. Therefore, we must be hard-working and patient, and have experience and be willing to take responsibility. You are all selected by the City Party Headquarters, and there are a few points you must remember: (1) You must fulfill your responsibility, do not perfunctorily handle things. You must understand that you must not disappoint the people. The City Party Headquarters is responsible to the people's groups, and you are responsible to the City Party Headquarters. If you cannot take responsibility, you can explain it first, do not delay the public, and become a public criminal. Do not think that being a literacy teacher is a small matter, have confidence, and do things well. Then we will not only benefit ourselves, but also benefit the country, society, and mankind, and our own spirit will be even more comforted. Our method of saving the country is to save the country from our own position, and everyone should fulfill their own responsibility. (2) You must have a spirit of service, and respond to the needs of the people you are teaching, such as the porter teams, etc. First, you must have a strong sense of empathy. Do not think of yourself as an educator, appearing dignified and putting on a teacher's airs. Second, life must be hard. Do not think that you can live a life of luxury. Third, you must have a missionary spirit. Only then will you be qualified as a literacy teacher.

Report: (1) You must recruit students and find school locations yourself. Regardless of whether you hope for Type A (70 or more people), Type B (50 or more people), or Type C (30 or more people), recruitment is entirely up to you. The scale and results depend on your own efforts. The number of people in the morning and afternoon classes can be calculated on average. (3) Not only teach literacy, but also teach knowledge and guide civic training, that is, supplement teaching when teaching characters. (4) Teacher's salary (A) calculated from the opening day of the school, (B) Type A salary 30 yuan, miscellaneous expenses 5 yuan (if miscellaneous expenses are not needed, this 5 yuan will be added to the teacher's salary), Type B salary 25 yuan, Type C 20 yuan (Type B and C miscellaneous expenses are the same as Type A), the remaining money is used to purchase paper and pens for students (estimated at 10 cents per student). At the end, if there is a shortage, the three types will be combined for calculation. If there is a surplus, prizes will be prepared.

(Preparation) (1) Before June 20, officially establish separately. From tomorrow (the 12th) to the 18th, complete preparations, and separately recruit locations and students. As long as it is within the scope of Shanghai, no matter where, it is roughly divided into (A) finding a region, (B) finding a house, and (C) recruiting students. (2) In advance, the City Party Headquarters has found permitted houses, etc. After the meeting, you can contact the staff of this association, it was said. The meeting adjourned at 4:30 p.m.

Ministry of Finance Instructs All Consolidated Tax Bureaus and Offices; Gansu Province Cigarette Secretly Handles Consolidated Tax

To be Implemented from July 1

The Ministry of Finance has decided that the consolidated tax on cigarettes in Gansu Province will be changed to be handled by the central government from July 1. Yesterday, it specially instructed all consolidated tax bureaus and offices, roughly stating that the preparatory work for the consolidated tax on cigarettes in Gansu Province has been temporarily approved by this department for trial implementation. It is planned that from the 24th year, the central government will allocate supplementary funds to subsidize local education and various legitimate purposes. From July 1 of this year, all cigarettes in Gansu Province will be subject to consolidated tax. All cigarettes leaving the factory in provinces implementing consolidated tax and transported to Gansu Province shall pay consolidated tax, affix sufficient stamps, and obtain a consolidated tax transportation permit before being allowed to be transported. After the cigarettes arrive in Gansu Province, no additional taxes or levies shall be imposed to comply with tax policy. After the consolidated tax is implemented this time, cigarettes originally stored in Shaanxi Province that applied to be transported to Gansu Province because the cigarettes transported to Gansu Province took the route through Shaanxi Province, resulting in the collection of transit taxes, shall not apply to the ministry for tax refunds to seek advantage, etc.

Beautiful Hull: The ship is 260 feet long, 50 feet wide, and has a draft of 9 feet 6 inches. Its speed is approximately 12 nautical miles per hour or more. The machinery was custom-made by a famous Swiss factory. The hull was decorated at the company's own factory in Hong Kong. There are a total of 20 dining rooms, with half of them being single rooms and half of them being double rooms. The first-class cabin can accommodate 22 people, and the steerage can accommodate 80 people. The decoration of each part is magnificent, the air circulation is good, and water coolers and electric fans are provided, making it warm in winter and cool in summer. The deck is spacious, allowing passengers to take a walk. Other advantages are too numerous to mention.

City Chamber of Commerce Cables Ministry of Finance to Request Restoration of Stamp Duty Review Committee

Yesterday, the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce cabled the Ministry of Finance in Nanjing, stating that after the Ministry of Finance's legal institutions依法审罚依法审罚 and implemented it for several months, merchants have felt quite obstructed: (1) The court already handles many cases on a regular basis, and now that it has to handle stamp duty violation cases, it is inevitable that it will be overwhelmed. According to merchants, it takes two to three months to complete a case. When the case is not completed, the seized account books cannot be returned according to regulations. However, the relationship between account books and business is also delayed day by day, which is the most inconvenient thing for merchants. (2) The court has few precedents for the Ministry's orders and decisions on stamp duty matters, and it is inevitable that there will be discrepancies in handling unfamiliar cases. Although the ruling can still be appealed, the court's three-level, three-trial system will soon be implemented. Now that stamp duty cases are handled by the primary trial, they will be handled by the local trial court in the future. For cases ruled by the Shanghai Local Court, it will be necessary to appeal to the Suzhou Higher Court in the future, so the cost of litigation for a case with a fine of ten yuan will be several times higher, which is extremely inconvenient. Therefore, due to these two difficulties, it is generally believed that stamp duty cases are originally administrative penalties. Except for the concessions, which can only maintain the current system due to special circumstances, it is more appropriate to restore the former Stamp Duty Review Committee in other inland areas. Since the association has the responsibility to convey commercial information, it does not dare to withhold it from the higher authorities. It is reasonable to cable and request the Ministry to review and approve the implementation for public convenience. Respectfully, the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce.

Report on the Income of the Chinese and Foreign Relief Society

The Current Situation of Disaster Relief and Famine in Liyang

The Chinese and Foreign Relief Society on Renji Road has successively completed the spring relief work in various districts of Jiangsu Province that have been severely affected by the drought. However, the disaster area in Liyang is vast and the disaster situation is even more serious. It is working with the Jisheng Society, so it is still investigating and providing relief. The report of the commissioner sent by the society is copied as follows: Liyang has always been known as a wealthy area, but it has been repeatedly affected by famine and military disasters. The financial sector has long been severely damaged. In addition, there was a severe drought last year. All the mountain and embankment fields in the county, totaling more than 1 million mu, were completely cracked after the summer, and the rivers were completely cracked. Districts 12364 of the county have been surveyed as soon as possible. Among them, the disaster situation in Districts 3 and 6 is the most serious. The reason is that the terrain is high and there are many mountains. It was dry before the drought and barren before the barrenness, so it is especially severe compared to other districts. The terrain in Districts 1 and 2 is slightly flatter, and people's livelihoods are slightly more active, but the disaster situation is the same. When investigating in various villages, I personally saw that the general disaster victims were thin and haggard, and dying people were everywhere. When entering their villages, no chickens or dogs could be heard. When entering their rooms, there was nothing. The misery is beyond description. Many people died from digging and eating Guanyin flour (tender stone), which caused abdominal pain, difficulty in defecation, and constipation. Many people also ate grass roots and bark. Because District 6 was more severely affected, it was investigated first. On May 28 and 29, relief rice was distributed at the Baoen Temple in the county seat. A total of 1,472 tickets for 2 dou of rice, 3,577 tickets for 3 dou of rice, and 1,413 tickets for 4 dou of rice were collected, and a total of 1,932 dan and 7 dou of relief rice were distributed. When distributing relief, the county magistrate was invited to supervise the distribution in the name of this association and the Jisheng Society, and party, government, military, and police personnel attended the event to assist. Xu from the Wuxi Catholic Church also came to Liyang to help. Districts 2 and 3 have also been surveyed successively. District 2 is divided into 22 villages. A total of 9,662 households have been issued relief tickets. The code words on the relief tickets are the five characters "Hui Jian Miao Zheng Guo." The distribution is being planned in a unified manner. Now that it is the season of Mangzhong, the wheat harvest is approaching. Although the farmers have a slight celebration of the harvest, they must plant rice seedlings immediately. It is heard that many people lack rice seeds. About one-quarter of the white fields in each village can be seen. The planted seedlings are gradually withering due to the hot weather and lack of ponds and rivers, which makes irrigation difficult. If there is no rain for a week, the planted seedlings will inevitably wither.

Family Members of Sailors on the Lexington Ship Petitioned Various Agencies Yesterday

Personally Submitting a Petition Stating the Guarantee Process and Requesting Justice and a Thorough Investigation of False Accusations

Regarding the unclear death of sailor He Baosheng, who served on the Lexington ship, the deceased's wife, He Zhuxingyu, personally requested relief from the union. In addition, four sailors from the Lexington ship, Tu Decai, etc., were investigated by the union without any suspicious points being found. Furthermore, the Yanying General Agency and other maritime groups, as well as another real commercial firm, provided a guarantee, requesting that they be allowed to temporarily serve on the ship and await investigation. However, after Tu and others returned to the ship, it was mistakenly heard that they were bailed out by union staff, and that Tu and others were temporarily returning to work on the ship meant that they were going to escape. It was not understood that the detectives at the time were only conducting inquiries and were not arresting them. Therefore, the union was able to move to the union for inquiries. After the inquiry, no suspicious points were found, and the guarantee was allowed based on the efforts of the group. They were allowed to temporarily return to the ship and await investigation. Now it is learned that the wives and all the sailors of the ship, as well as their families in Shanghai, have for days heard that someone is making false accusations and creating rumors, which is obviously malicious. Outraged, they specially requested the Yanying General Agency and other maritime groups to lead them to petition the party, government, and military agencies in the city yesterday, personally submitting a petition proving that Tu Decai and others were indeed falsely accused and that there were obviously villains at work, requesting a thorough investigation to clarify the injustice and maintain justice. The details and petition are recorded below:

Petition Situation: Yesterday, there were a total of more than 400 family members of sailors on the Lexington ship, men and women mixed, young and old, in a very miserable situation. At 8 a.m., led by the Yanying General Agency and other maritime groups, they took seven large trucks to the City Party Headquarters, the Municipal Government, the Security Department, the Municipal Public Security Bureau, the Maritime Union, the Maritime Party and Township Association, and other places to petition. They were all received by the main personnel, who expressed sympathy for the points of the petition, and promised to thoroughly investigate and uphold justice in addition to comfort, it was said.

Petition: We are here to report that someone is intending to extort money and make false accusations. Please investigate thoroughly to clarify the injustice and maintain justice. The circumstances of the unclear death of sailor He Baosheng on the Lexington ship are unclear. The wives of Tu Decai, Jiang Fucai, Chen Yuebei, and Le A'er were interrogated and detained for two days by the Public Security Avoidance Detective Team on the day the ship arrived in port. They were not informed of the reason. The ship was about to sail, and Tu and Jiang were the leaders of the firemen and watermen. If they missed the ship because of this, not only would Tu and Jiang's livelihood be cut off, but all the workers on the ship would lose their jobs. The wives were extremely panic-stricken and begged the Yanying General Agency and other five maritime groups to petition the Maritime Union for relief. The Maritime Union sent personnel to negotiate with the Public Security Bureau, which stated that it was an inquiry and not an arrest. Therefore, the Maritime Union held a letter and moved the inquiry to the union. After strict questioning by the union, it was determined that Tu and others had no suspicious points. Therefore, the Yanying General Agency and other five maritime groups and the Shanghai National Trading Company guaranteed that they would return to the ship, temporarily work, and await investigation. The officials of the Shaoxing Native Place Association had other intentions and did not achieve their wishes. After Tu and others returned to the ship, they made a big fuss, with sinister intentions, determined to achieve their wish to frame them. The staff of the Shaoxing Native Place Association went to the Maritime Union to request relief after Tu and others returned to the ship. The union explained the case and comforted them. Later, they also expressed gratitude and left, and presented a petition to the union for relief the next day. After a few days, the Shaoxing Native Place Association falsely claimed that Tu and other four people were suspects, creating rumors and lending this as an excuse to arrange for others to take their positions, so that they could profit from it. The two accounts were contradictory, as if it were a child's play, confusing the audience, and the situation was obviously bad. Tu and other four people were usually careful and prudent and had never committed any wrongdoing. The whole ship praised them. They were unjustly wronged. Fortunately, the union was discerning and knew that they were innocent, and also considered their livelihoods and allowed them to temporarily be released on bail to return to work on the ship and await investigation. The families were able to rely on them for their livelihood and avoid displacement. They were grateful for the bright virtue and were all willing to die for it. They were deeply disappointed by the various slanders of the staff of the Shaoxing Native Place Association (omitted below).

Ningbo Native Place Association Hopes That the Temporary Tax on the Fishing Industry on Shengsi Island Will Be Abolished

The Ningbo Native Place Association in Shanghai stated that the residents of the Chongming County Fifth District Shengsi Islands are all from Zhejiang and engaged in the fishing industry. The county's business tax bureau recently set up offices on the Shengsi Islands to levy a temporary business tax on the fishing industry. The association believes that Shengsi is a fish-producing area. All the fish caught must be transported to other ports for sale and must bear business tax. It is inevitable that levying taxes at the place of origin is a superimposed structure. It has separately telegraphed the Jiangsu Provincial Government and the Ministry of Finance to express its opinions. Now that the case is unresolved, it has sent a special letter to the Fifth District Office of Chongming County asking it to advocate for unity. The letter states: "Respected Sir, the Chongming County Business Tax Bureau has levied a temporary business tax on the fishing industry on the Shengsi Islands under the jurisdiction of the Fifth District, with a tax rate of 0.5% for both fishermen and fish merchants. It is heard that items such as fish salt, fishing gear, and baked hemp are also subject to taxation. Shengsi Islands are fish-producing areas. The result of fishing by fishermen (such as fishing boats, etc.) and fish merchants' activities (such as ice boats, etc.) must be transported to Shanghai, Ningbo, Hangzhou, Shaoxing, and ports along the Yangtze River for sale. At that time, the local business tax bureau will naturally levy taxes. Now, if a temporary business tax is levied at the place of origin, it seems that it is inevitable that it is a superimposed tax. This year, the price of fish has plummeted, and fishermen and fish merchants are all on the verge of bankruptcy. Imposing a heavy tax on them will put the fishing industry in a state of irretrievable disaster. Our association is currently submitting separate requests to the Ministry of Industry and Commerce, the Ministry of Finance, and the Jiangsu Provincial Government to prevent this. Your district office is stationed there and must have heard of the difficult situation. Therefore, we are writing to ask you to advocate for unity in order to maintain a lifeline for the fishing industry."

Shanghai Conference of the Christian Faith and Action Salvation Corps; First Use Written Advice for Suicide Cases

The China Christian Faith and Action Salvation Corps, based on the Christian gospel and its spirit of universal love, sacrifice, and saving the world, aims to assist the church in promoting the truth and to awaken the Chinese people to engage in reforming hearts, saving people, and saving the country. It has established a general headquarters in the capital. After the establishment of the Shanghai Regional Corps, the number of members reached more than 380. The elected executive committee members are Zhu Guishen, Li Denghui, Zhang Zhijiang, Zhao Jinqing, Kong Yongzhi, Wu Xiaogu, Yao Xianyang, Yu Zhizhai, Xue Ziliang, Wang Wanzhi, Dong Jing'an, Wang Rutang, Xie Songgao, You Shuzhu, Chen Jinyong, Zhu Baoluo, Jin Yanqing, Wei Shaozeng, Shao Yunqing, Wang, and Weng Guoxun, etc., more than 20 people. Xie Songsan, Ma Shuguan, Hong Kunshan, Zhu Haoran, Zhou Meicun, etc. were in the minority of five. Yesterday afternoon, the third first executive committee meeting was held at the office at No. 316 Xizang Road. Mr. Yu Zhizhai was appointed as the temporary chairman. After the ceremony, the staff reported on the progress of the regional corps and the process of hosting the National Congress of Representatives in Shanghai. Zhao Jinqing was elected as the chairman, and Mr. Zhu Guishen and Mr. You Shuxun were elected as the vice chairmen. Li Denghui was elected as the economic committee member, and Yu Zhizhai was elected as the document committee member. Next, the committee discussed the resignation requests of the four executive committee members and decided to express sincere retention. In addition to urging them in writing, they also asked the attendees to persuade them separately. Zhao Jinqing proposed that suicide cases in Shanghai are increasing day by day, and even the whole family is destroyed, which is unbearable to hear. The corps is based on the principle of saving people and should take measures to eliminate it. It is proposed to first use written advice and should be publicly decided, which was unanimously approved. You Shuxun was designated as the drafter and was given a time limit to publish it soon. Then, they had lunch and dispersed.

Longhua Temple Restoration: The Imperial Edition of the Great Buddhist Canon of the Wanli Era of the Ming Dynasty

Preliminary Sorting Reveals Losses; Temple Resolves to Copy and Supplement to Complete the Volume

According to the Datong News Agency, the ancient Longhua Temple in this city, built during the Three Wu Dynasties, houses in its Sutra Repository a complete imperial edition of the Great Buddhist Canon from the Wanli period of the Ming Dynasty. The temple's abbot, Xing Kong, considering this canon to be of great importance to Chinese literature, and not to be treated lightly, decided to restore it. However, preliminary examination revealed that it had been partially lost. Details are as follows:

Brief Account of the Sutra Repository

The complete Great Buddhist Canon is arranged with thirteen volumes per case, excluding the table of contents, totaling 730 cases. This time, the temple's abbot, Xing Kong, invited Master Mantu to conduct a preliminary sorting. Upon inspection, 355 cases were found to be complete and undamaged, 319 cases were partially damaged, and 53 cases were completely lost.

Regrettable Losses

The case numbers of the completely lost sections are: Xuan, Sheng, Kun, Nai, Qian, Diao, Tang, Chui, Ping, Zhang, Ju, Shi, Wu, Nv, Liang, Si, Jing, Ke, Zheng, Fei Yue, Liu, Shi, Shan, Bie, Feng, You, Yi, Mi, Nei, Jie, Bing, Chi, Ce, Ying, Kuang, You, Duo, Meng, Jian, Heng, Ting, Jia, Bao, Yi, Jue, Jia, You, Mian, Tai, Jiao, She, totaling 53 cases.

Destroyed by Cixi

Master Mantu, who was invited to undertake the restoration of the canon at Longhua Temple, has extensive experience in sutra sorting. In 1930, when Chongqing Huayan Temple requested a copy of the Great Buddhist Canon from Beiping, Master Mantu was responsible for proofreading it. That canon was also a Ming edition, but regrettably, five cases, Yi, Jue, Jia, You, and Mian, were destroyed by Empress Dowager Cixi of the Qing Dynasty, also not being a complete set.

Copying and Supplementation Planned

Abbot Xing Kong of Longhua Temple plans to copy and supplement the lost and damaged sections after the entire canon has been sorted, in order to create a complete volume. However, the work is extensive and will require Master Mantu to oversee the entire process to preserve the literature.

There is a garbage dump at the rear of No. 3 San Guantang Road, just off of South Shanghai's Lujiabang Road. Additionally, to the east end of San Guantang and the east end of Liyuan Road's Dabu Assembly Hall there is an area used to defecate and urinate at will. Lawyers Should Not Abuse Advertisements

The Shanghai Bar Association sent a letter yesterday to members who had published advertisements in the Da Ri Bao newspaper. It reads, "We write to inform you that, to rectify discipline, we notified all members on October 29th of last year that, regarding newspaper advertisements, aside from representing clients, announcing the relocation of offices, changes in telephone numbers, or commencing practice, and celebratory messages, one should not independently publish advertisements resembling the solicitation of lawsuits, or merely list names, offices, and telephone numbers. Recently, however, it has come to our attention that the names and telephone numbers of your members have continued to appear in advertisements in the Da Ri Bao, raising suspicions of violating resolutions and disrupting discipline. The 197th Joint Meeting of the Executive and Supervisory Committees of the Association has resolved to send a letter instructing the cessation of such advertisements. We hereby notify you to investigate and promptly cease publishing such advertisements to avoid misunderstandings."

Fire Burns Five Houses in Sipailou Within the City

Yang Henglong Robe and Costume Shop, No. 43 Sipailou Road, inside the East Gate, is owned by Yang Jianqing from Suzhou. Yang's family lives upstairs. For over twenty years, they have employed Ye Songru from Zhenjiang as an accountant, Xia Qingyun, and others as staff, along with seven apprentices. The business is doing well. The shop next door, No. 41, Xintai Xiang Shroud Shop, is owned by Gu Zhiren from Haiyan, and has been there for three years. The two shops share a two-story rear building. Unexpectedly, at 2:50 AM yesterday, a fire suddenly broke out in the firewood room in the rear building. The fire quickly spread through the rice straw and became uncontrollable. Pan Ruan, a Zhenjiang worker sleeping in the Yang Henglong parlor, discovered the fire and shouted a warning. Everyone was startled awake and immediately reported it to Zhu Zidan, the police officer at Post No. 10 of the Yimiao Police Station of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, who used the telephone to notify various fire brigades to dispatch fire engines to the scene quickly. However, the fire was raging fiercely and had already broken through the roof. After the firefighters worked tirelessly to extinguish the flames, the fire was finally brought under control after about two hours. Five houses were destroyed, and the loss of goods was considerable. The police station dispatched several officers to maintain order and investigate the cause of the fire, taking Yang Jianqing and Gu Zhiren to the station for questioning. It is reported that Yang Henglong did not have fire insurance, while Xintai Xiang had fire insurance for 3,000 yuan with Huaxing Insurance.

Shanghai-Guangdong Long-Distance Telephone: Trial Call Successful; Construction of Iron Supports Underway; Official Call Service to Begin October 1st

The Shanghai-Guangdong long-distance wireless telephone, with the Shanghai equipment already installed and the Guangdong project nearing completion, has recently undergone trial calls, which have been quite successful. Both stations are now rushing to construct the iron supports under the antennas, with the official opening of the call service expected on October 1st of this year. The details are as follows:

Shanghai Equipment Now Installed

The Shanghai-Guangdong long-distance wireless telephone project, after several discussions between the Ministry of Communications and the Guangdong Provincial Government, saw Guangdong send Deng Zongyao, the chairman of the Guangdong Provincial Automatic Telephone Management Committee and director of the Guangzhou Telephone Bureau, to Shanghai for negotiations. Deng also escorted construction materials back to Guangdong. According to the agreed construction plan, both sides began work. Shanghai designated Zhenru as the main telephone station. After the International Telecommunications Bureau began construction, which has taken several months, it is reported that all equipment has now been installed. The installation of the iron supports under the antennas is currently underway. This project will take two months to complete.

Guangdong Project Mostly Complete

The Guangdong telephone station was also selected at Shipai. Since the China Electric Company, which contracted the project, began construction in cooperation with the Guangdong Provincial Department of Construction and the Municipal Government, the project has progressed rapidly and is mostly complete. The required equipment has also been purchased in England by the Wu Geng Material Procurement Committee and shipped to Guangdong. The installation of the iron supports is also currently underway.

Trial Call Held, Results Satisfactory

With the equipment installation on both sides completed, a trial call was immediately held. The results were quite satisfactory. It is understood that the equipment is extremely complex and will require several more trial calls. The official opening date will be October 1st, as the iron support project under the antennas is extensive and will take two months to complete.

Thunderstorm Yesterday Afternoon Sparks Unfounded Rumors; No Cases of Electrocution or Shattered Rocks Found Upon Investigation

Yesterday afternoon at 4:40 PM, the sky was overcast and threatening rain. Suddenly, there was a flash of lightning and a crash of thunder, but no rain fell. After the thunder, rumors spread that someone had been electrocuted near the Little West Gate. The news spread quickly, and many people flocked to the area to find out what had happened, causing crowds to gather near Shangwen and Zhonghua Roads in the Little West Gate area. In reality, nothing had happened. Police officers stationed around the area, fearing trouble, worked hard to maintain traffic, but the crowds only grew larger. Then, rumors spread that lightning had struck a millstone. It was said that a broken millstone was outside the house (located on Xueqian Street) of Zhou Zenglu, a local resident who owns a rice shop at No. 100 Shangwen Road, Little West Gate. A square blue stone was also mentioned. The crowds claimed that the stone had been shattered by lightning. To verify the truth, a reporter entered the premises and observed that the cracks in the millstone were filled with dirt, indicating that they were old. The blue stone was intact. The story of the lightning-struck millstone was entirely a rumor. Even by evening, groups of people were still wandering around, peering about. It was a case of needless alarm.
