Threw Bag of Excrement During "White Snake" Performance: Sixth Grader Takes Revenge, Wu Ma and Others Suffer Unpleasant Taste

—Sentenced to Three Months Imprisonment—

The Huaiyang Grand Theater at No. 158 Wuzhou Road has been performing "The Tale of the White Snake" recently, and business has been good. On the 7th of this month, Gao, a sixth grader from Jiangbei, attempted to watch the performance without purchasing a ticket and was ejected by the ticket inspector. Gao harbored resentment and sought revenge. On the evening of the 8th, he went to see the performance again, sitting in the fifth row of the upper level. At 11:10 PM, during the scene where the real and fake White Snakes were battling, it was necessary to completely extinguish the theater's lights. Gao saw this as his opportunity and threw a package of yellowish-white matter he had brought with him downwards. It landed on the bodies of audience members Wu Ma, Wu Xiaolan, Jiang Zhu, and Gu Jin, covering them in excrement and causing them to experience an unpleasant taste. Fortunately, the theater's deputy manager, Wu Tingzhi, was nearby when Gao threw the excrement and immediately apprehended him. Detective Xu Zhiqing and the police arrived and took Gao into custody at the Jiaxing Road Police Station, before sending him to Criminal Division V of the First Special District Court. Judge Ye Shengchao opened the court and questioned him. Detective Division lawyer Li Zhishan stated the case, charging him under Article 319 of the Criminal Code. Considering the reprehensible nature of the act, he requested a severe sentence to deter others. The victims, Wu Ma and others, then testified about the incident. Gao confessed to throwing the excrement, claiming he was instructed to do so by Da Pubao Lao Hai and others. Judge Ye, after considering the evidence, sentenced Gao to three months imprisonment as a warning.

It could only be confirmed after the original owner identified it. President Feng granted the detective division's request and ordered the jewelry to be temporarily stored in the detective division.

A Planned Conspiracy: Tying Up a Man and Woman and Falsely Accusing Them of Adultery - Yang Lansheng's Vicious Plot to Divorce His Wife - Fortunately, His Daughter Saw What Happened and Reported It to the Police, Revealing the Inside Story

Yang Lansheng, a local resident aged thirty-six, who works as a cook in the Wan Zai military camp on Chengdu Road, married Cai more than ten years ago and lives with her at No. 7, Qijiacun, Tokyo Road, Shanghai West. During the day, the couple's relationship is considered harmonious, and they have a daughter named A'e, who is already fourteen years old. However, recently, the Yangs have become suspicious of each other. The husband accuses his wife of committing adultery with a neighbor from Changzhou, Chen Yusheng, while the wife accuses her husband of taking another concubine, leading to frequent quarrels and a breakdown in their relationship. They are incompatible, and Yang sees Cai as a thorn in his side, constantly thinking of ways to harm her so that he can find an excuse to divorce her. He discussed this with a friend known as "Old Matchmaker," and they decided to take drastic measures. At 4:50 AM on the 9th of this month, as dawn was breaking, seven or eight men in short clothes suddenly broke into Chen Yusheng's house in Qijiacun, tied up Chen's hands and feet with ropes, and stuffed paper into his mouth to prevent him from making any noise. Then they took Chen to the nearby Yang Cai's house and went straight into Cai's bedroom. These people first threw Chen onto Cai's bed and then tied up Cai as well, placing her on the same bed. They also intended to strip Cai of her clothes and then inform Cai's husband, Yang Lansheng, pretending to have caught them in the act of adultery, so that he could use this as grounds for divorce. This plan was all prearranged. Unexpectedly, Cai's daughter, Yang A'e, was horrified by the scene and rushed out to report it to the Putuo Road Police Station. The station dispatched several Chinese and foreign detectives who rushed to the scene and arrested five people on the spot: Chen Zhaorong, Xi Aliuli, Nie Rongbiao, Gong Housheng, and Zhang Hengshao. They also untied Yang Cai and Chen Yusheng, removed the paper from their mouths, and took them all to the police station. Later, Yang Lansheng was apprehended on Laobosen Road. Yesterday morning, they were all sent to the Eighth Criminal Court of the First Special Court. In addition to prosecuting them according to Articles 316 and 230 of the Criminal Law, the police station's lawyer, Qian Xunjiu, also stated the above situation. Subsequently, Yang Cai and Chen Yusheng filed a case, proving that they were forcibly tied up by the defendants and accused of adultery. They also stated that they did not know each other and were falsely accused. When questioned, the defendants admitted to the accusations. After Judge Liu Yugui verified the confession, he ordered that the case be adjourned and retried this Friday.

After the Yongxing Money Shop Closed Down - The New Culture Press Sues - For Owed Debts of Over 24,000 Yuan - Sues All Shareholders for Joint Debt Settlement

The Jiangnan Bank was founded by Yu Zhendong and others, with Yu serving as the president. During this Dragon Boat Festival, it became difficult to overcome difficulties, and it has already announced the suspension of business due to insufficient capital turnover. In addition to running the bank, Yu also jointly opened the Yongxing Money Shop with Chen Jingtao, Chen Dizhou, Guo Ruoyu, Chen Zhongchi, Chen Meibo, and others, with Chen Jingtao serving as the manager. The shop also fell victim to the current economic crisis and closed down before Jiangnan Bank. The amount of debt it owes is very large. Now, the creditor, New Culture Press, has hired lawyer Chen Tingrui to file a lawsuit against all the shareholders of Yongxing Shop, including Yu Zhendong, Chen Jingtao, Chen Dizhou, Guo Ruoyu, Chen Zhongchi, and Chen Meibo. The lawsuit states that Yongxing was jointly opened by the defendants, with Chen Jingtao as the manager. The plaintiff originally had no dealings with them. In February of this year, the defendants suddenly sent their street salesman, Shao Xianglin, to persuade them to deposit funds, boasting about how stable and reliable they were. The plaintiff then successively deposited 24,600 yuan, holding a passbook as proof. Last month, they needed to withdraw a portion of the funds, and the shop issued a bill for 14,280 yuan. However, when it came time to cash it on April 20th, the business was already closed. For more than a month now, they have entrusted people to liquidate the assets, but the matter has been delayed repeatedly. They have ignored both the bill and the remaining deposit of 10,320 yuan. It is found that the defendants are partners of Yongxing and wealthy merchants in Shanghai, and they should bear joint and several liability for the debts. Recently, the Ministry of Finance has repeatedly issued orders that shareholders of bankrupt money shops should be fully liable for repayment. Otherwise, not only will individual assets be affected, but the social economy will also be disrupted. Therefore, they specially request a judgment ordering the repayment of the full amount plus interest. If the shop's assets are insufficient to cover the debt, then the defendants should be ordered to jointly repay it. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Shen Hong of the First Special District Court opened the court to summon and interrogate the defendants, but none of them appeared. The plaintiff's agent, Fan Chun, and his lawyer, Chen Tingrui, presented the reasons for the lawsuit. The court then ordered that the defendants be summoned to appear at a later date for further interrogation.

Shanghai Vocational Youth Life Improvement Association - Mao Zhenchu and Others Initiate Organization

Mao Zhenchu, secretary and director of general affairs of the Shanghai Silk Industry Bank, Guo Chongjie, editor-in-chief of the Shanghai Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, and others, considering the large number of young people serving in the vocational sector in Shanghai, numbering in the tens of thousands, who have no organization and are unable to improve themselves, and given the current social instability, are generally experiencing depression in their lives. This depression in life leads to either extreme hedonism or complete negativity. Not only are the vocational youths themselves lifeless, but they will also be on the path to destruction. The losses to the country and society are even greater. Vocational youths are distributed in all aspects of society, and their position in society is worthy of cherishing. If they do not strive for self-improvement, it will make the turbulent society even more unstable. Therefore, more than one hundred vocational youths jointly initiated the organization of the "Shanghai Vocational Youth Life Improvement Association." Based on the principle of self-help and helping others, they have been supported by people from all walks of life, including Pan Gongzhan, Wang Yansong, Yang Weiyu, Xiang Kangyuan, and Jia Foru. Last month, a general meeting of initiators was convened, and the declaration and draft charter were passed on the spot. Mao Zhenchu, Wang Jianmin, He Jingyu, Guo Chongjie, Gongsun Min, Chen Guanlin, Cheng Keguang, Wang Qixu, and Hu Weijian were elected as nine preparatory committee members responsible for carrying out the work. They have received a certificate of permission to establish the association from the Municipal Party Headquarters and will convene a general meeting soon to formally announce its establishment. The current address of the association is Room 311, Silk Industry Building, East Shilu, Hankou Road. It is said that they are currently publicly soliciting members. Any vocational youth in the city can join by stating their name, age, place of service, address, and other information. The origin and work outline of the association are recorded as follows:

Origin: We and others serve in Shanghai. Although our occupations are not entirely the same, we have common feelings. This is the depression in life and the hunger for knowledge. Since we left school and entered society, all aspects of our material and spiritual life, such as clothing, food, housing, transportation, knowledge, hygiene, and friendship, are far from our ideals. At first, we resisted, but eventually, we were assimilated by the environment and fell into a deep abyss of decadence and depression. Looking at the future, we cannot help but feel apprehensive. Therefore, there is the initiation of the "Shanghai Vocational Youth Life Improvement Association." However, our knowledge and ability are limited. The development of this association depends on the enthusiastic participation of like-minded people. Therefore, we use the meaning of the birds chirping to seek friends to work together. We respectfully state the origin to be the starting point. May our comrades consider it. All organizational matters will be handled in accordance with legal procedures and will be absolutely open. We hope that all comrades who join will give full play to their high opinions and help with great efforts so that the association's affairs can progress daily.

Outline: (A. Knowledge Aspect) (1) Establish a counseling department: 1. Publish publications; 2. Organize symposiums; 3. Provide correspondence answers to all questions. (2) Run practical schools: 1. Initially contact the more well-established vocational supplementary schools already operating in the city to become special schools of the association and provide members with preferential admission; 2. Gradually run our own schools when funds are sufficient. (3) Lectures: Hold systematic lectures on vocational studies and self-cultivation at any time. (4) Establish a library: Intend to gradually expand it and become a treasure trove of knowledge that ordinary vocational youths cannot live without for a day. (B. Economic Aspect) (1) Establish a counseling department: Provide members with guidance and planning for personal economic income and expenditure, and provide instructions on methods of economic management or use. (2) Organize savings: 1. Initially contact reliable banks and subscribe to special preferential contracts to facilitate members' savings at any time, thereby promoting thrift and preventing future problems; 2. Operate independently after conducting economic credit cooperation. (3) Promote insurance: 1. Life insurance; 2. Property insurance (including all income-generating renovations, houses, etc.); 3. Unemployment insurance. 1. Initially, contact reliable and well-managed insurance companies and subscribe to special group contracts to facilitate members' insurance at any time; 2. Operate independently after conducting economic credit cooperation. (4) Personal credit loans: The steps for implementation are the same as for organizing savings. (5) Consumer cooperatives: 1. Clothing; 2. Food; 3. Housing; 4. Transportation. All are based on the principles of economy and using domestic products, making full use of existing domestic industrial and commercial factories, companies, and transportation agencies to reduce the burden on members, and operating our own cooperatives to serve members. (C. Marriage Aspect) (1) Establish guidance: Provide face-to-face or correspondence instructions on all practical issues related to marriage. (2) Promote frugal weddings and take solemnity and economy as the principles of wedding ceremonies. (3) Provide design and planning for the allocation of marriage expenses and design economical and artistic homes. (D. Occupational Aspect) (1) Find ways to resolve occupational difficulties. (2) Guide occupational knowledge and skills. (E. Health Aspect) (1) Entertainment facilities: Including the following items: 1. Drama; 2. Chess; 3. Music; 4. Photography; 5. Travel. (2) Hygiene facilities: Including the following items: 1. Various sports equipment, ball games, and national arts, etc.; 2. Bathrooms; 3. Medical guidance and reduced or free medication, etc.

Jiande Bank Rent Dispute - Auctioning Branch Assets to Repay

Since Jiande Bank announced its liquidation last year, it was recently sued by Fu Zengkang, the representative of Zhicheng Real Estate Company, the landlord of the Hongqiao branch, for violating the lease contract. The case has been seized by the Shanghai Local Court. The appeal period has expired, and the plaintiff, accompanied by the clerk, went to the scene to auction the assets. A Mr. Yang purchased the bank's productive assets for 404 yuan and withdrew the case from the court.

Family Suicide Case - Yue Lin Accused of Inciting Suicide - Nine-Year-Old Girl Who Was Rescued Summoned to Court - Old Yue's Tears Flow as He Begs the Judge for Mercy

Yue Lin, a 51-year-old Beiping native living on the third floor of the Peng Yulai cake shop at 171 Avenue Dubail in the French Concession, due to unemployment and economic pressure, swallowed raw opium with his wife, Wang, and their eight children on the evening of the 30th of last month. Yue himself took a lighter dose and did not die until the next morning. He went out to throw himself into the river and was rescued, only to discover the tragedy at home. His wife and three sons and two daughters died because they could not be saved. Only the nine-year-old girl, Xiaoyun, was sent to the hospital and rescued. The French police suspected Yue Lin of inciting suicide and sent him to the Second Special Court for interrogation and investigation. The details have been recorded in this newspaper. Yesterday morning, Wang Gangxu, the presiding judge of the Second Special Court's Criminal Division, and clerk Zheng Rong went to the First Criminal Court to interrogate him. First, Yao Zhaodi, the lawyer representing the police department, stated the case, saying that the defendant Yue Lin sent his four-month-old daughter to the Renji Nursery Hall at 4:00 PM on the 30th of the month. At about 6:00 PM, he returned home, and his wife and six children had already swallowed opium. At 9:00 PM, Yue and his wife also took poison at the same time. The police department cannot investigate the part about the six children taking poison. As for Yue's wife, Wang, the defendant is suspected of inciting or assisting in suicide. He is now being prosecuted in accordance with Article 290 of the Criminal Law and requests that he be interrogated and judged according to the law. Then, the detective in charge of this case, Yu Yutian, reported the investigation process and said that he had interrogated the rescued nine-year-old girl in the hospital, who said that the opium was ordered to be swallowed by her father. Please summon her daughter Xiaoyun for interrogation. At this point, Yue Lin's eldest son, Guangfu, brought his sister, Xiaoyun, to the case. Yue could not help but feel sad when he saw his children, and tears flowed down his face. The official asked Xiaoyun, but because she was young and did not understand, she could not answer. The police then questioned her, but she answered that she did not know anything. The official then questioned Yue Lin, who said that he did not know that his wife intended to commit suicide. However, he usually said that he did not want to be poor and ashamed. He did not know where she got the opium this time. When I took the little girl to the nursery and returned home, she said to me that the children had already taken poison, fearing that they would become beggars in the future. I also advised her that we still have ten or eight yuan to live on, and we should wait until there is no way to make a decision. Later, the children went upstairs to sleep, not noisy, not crying, not shouting in pain, and fell asleep. I really didn't discuss or conspire to commit suicide beforehand. Afterwards, my mind was confused, and this happened. I beg for mercy. The court also summoned Chen Dezhi (from Chongming), the second landlord of Yue's cake shop, as a witness to inquire about Yue's daily situation. Chen said that Yue rented my house, and the rent was six and a half yuan per month. I don't know how his situation is because he usually enters and exits through the back door. I only learned about the poisoning after receiving a message. At this point, the police department's lawyer, Yao, expressed his opinion, saying that based on the facts, the defendant had the determination to die together, but according to the regulations, he should be exempt from punishment. The official said that the point of the defendant sending the four-month-old girl to the nursery still needs to be investigated. He ordered that the case be adjourned and retried on the 15th, and the defendant will remain in custody for further instructions.

Hu Die to Return Triumphant - Lin Xuehuai Passes Away Yesterday - Willed Depleted After Lost Love and Entangled by Illness - Gaunt and Dark Remains, No Longer the Elegant Young Man of Yore

Central News Agency reports: Our country's movie actress Hu Die, after participating in the Soviet Union International Film Festival and traveling to various European countries, is about to return. Unexpectedly, Lin Xuehuai, who introduced her to the film industry and once pledged to be together for life, only to have the Xue Die marriage change, passed away. This is enough for those who pay attention to Xue Die to sigh. Hu Die will likely feel sorrow upon learning of this bad news overseas.

First Meeting of Xue Die: Lin Xuehuai was 34 years old, from Zhongshan, Guangdong. He was handsome and good at photography. He joined the Youlian Film Company founded by Chen Kangran, a director at the Yihua Film Company, as a professional member. He then met Hu Die. Because of her graceful and charming nature, he tried his best to introduce her to Youlian as an actress. This is when she entered the film industry. Lin initially starred in the "Tea Picking Girl" film at the Baihe Company. His first film at the Mingxing Company was "The Last Conscience." Then he co-starred with Hu Die in the "Autumn Fan Complaint," and Hu Die's reputation gradually rose. She then transferred to the Tianyi Company and then to Mingxing, to this day. According to Lin Xuehuai's brother-in-law, Zheng Jingan, to the Central News Agency reporter, Hu's parents married her to Lin because of his encouragement.

Engagement in the Ballroom: The Yuegong Ballroom on North Sichuan Road happened to open at this time. Lin and Hu held their engagement ceremony on the opening day. Many people from all walks of life attended, and a tea dance was held. At that time, Yuegong was quite outstanding among Shanghai ballrooms, and those who participated in this grand event can still talk about it with relish.

Sudden Marriage Change: Later, Hu Die's artistic career became increasingly successful, and her status gradually increased. Later, she was even selected as the so-called "Chinese Film Queen," while Lin was unsuccessful and frustrated. The difference in social status increased, and the discord between the two sexes became apparent. Thus, the Xue Die marriage change case arose. Many people in society know about this process. In the end, Lin lost the lawsuit, and the stimulation he received must have been very great.

After Lost Love: After Lin retired from the film industry, he relied on his photography skills to make a living. He set up Xuehuai Photography Studio behind the Xin Xin Company and then transferred it to others. He then went to Suzhou with several thousand yuan to set up Xuehuai Photography Studio at the entrance of Zouqian Palace Lane. His life was still not bad. However, not long after opening, it was sealed up because he lost the Xue Die lawsuit. Lin lost love with Die, and was affected by the bad environment afterwards. The stimulation must have been even more painful.

Developed Cancer: Years ago, Lin developed cancer in the cheekbone area due to depression. He suffered greatly. In June of last year, he went to the Red Cross Hospital for examination. At that time, his body was very good. The doctor said, "Your body should be better than it is now six months ago. Six months later, it will be weaker. Your life is only a year away." He then used radium needles for treatment and received seven radiotherapy sessions at Yangshupu Sacred Heart Hospital. After recovery, it relapsed in less than a month. He traveled around, but medical treatment was ineffective. He then came to Shanghai and rented a residence at No. 6 Yongqing Lane, Ailaige Road, French Concession, to recuperate.

Passed Away Yesterday Afternoon: At 3:15 PM yesterday afternoon, Lin passed away due to illness. He left behind his wife, Wang Peizhen, (a local, 24 years old, who was in a free love relationship and married for less than three years,) and a daughter, Meimei, (one year old). Lin's brother-in-law, Zheng Jingan, helped to handle the funeral arrangements and sent the body to the Chinese Funeral Home on Haige Road for embalming. The coffin will be placed on the 13th and the funeral will be held at 1:00 PM on the 14th. According to Zheng Jingan, Lin's finances were quite tight due to years of illness. However, he had many friends during his lifetime. Those who intend to carry the coffin should bring their own vehicles. The photography studio in Suzhou may be continued by his widow. The Central News Agency reporter once visited Lin's mortuary. Lin had already been made up and dressed in a long gown and mandarin jacket. However, his face was gaunt and dark, no longer the elegant young man of yore.

Autopsy of Flower Shop Apprentice Crushed to Death by Car - Private Prosecution Part Already Settled

Tan Yunxiang's youngest son, Longgen, a local resident living at No. 91 Kongjiaqiao, Jixifeier Road, Public Concession, is sixteen years old this year. He has been an apprentice at the Guba Flower Shop at No. 124 Guba Road, French Concession, for four years. He is intelligent and capable, so he is deeply valued by the shop owner. He is in charge of all the shop's affairs. On the evening of the 3rd of this month, Longgen was free and riding a bicycle for recreation. At 9:20 PM, he rode his bicycle out of Lane 156 of Guba Road and turned east. At that time, a car No. 18566 of Xiangsheng Motor Company, driven by Zhang Acai (23 years old), was speeding south on Guba Road. He failed to brake and avoid it, causing Tan Longgen to be knocked down with his bicycle, and his abdomen and left leg were scratched by the iron bar under the car. The police saw this, recorded the number, and took the injured person and the car to the Fuxu Police Station. The injured person was sent to Guangci Hospital, where doctors performed surgery and treatment, but he died of his injuries at 9:00 PM the day before yesterday. The hospital notified the police station, and the body was carried to the Tongren Fuyuan Funeral Home for an autopsy. Yesterday, the police station reported to the Special Court, and Prosecutor Wang Ren, forensic doctor Jiang Xuan, and clerk Zhao Yifen went to the funeral home to examine the body. They sat in public and questioned the defendant Zhang Acai and witnesses about the accident. The body was handed over to Tan Yunxiang, who applied to collect the body for burial. The official examined and found that Tan Longgen had been injured by a car and died. The body was collected by the family. Whether the defendant was negligent will be investigated and dealt with by the police department. It is heard that the police station investigated the negligence and found that it was due to the deceased. As for the private prosecution for compensation, the defendant has asked someone to mediate a settlement with the family of the deceased and compensated 300 yuan to close the case.

Pawned White Silk Switched Case - Two Criminals Detained Awaiting Sentencing

On October 16th at 11:15 AM, Zhou Xingshun and Li Aqing, from Ningbo, went to the Yuandian Pawnshop at No. 182 Wuzhou Road to pawn white silk worth five yuan. They used a switching trick to fraudulently obtain money and divide the loot. After the case was discovered, they were arrested by Chinese detective Zhou Yushan and detective Ma Binggui. The investigation revealed that they had used the same method to defraud more than 20 pawnshops, including Qiande at No. 296 Zhoujiazhulu, Fujia at No. 40 Fanjialu, Yongkang at No. 259 Oujialu, Baoyuan at No. 231 Donghan Bili Road, and Xiechang at No. 510 Haining Road, of more than 70 yuan. They were sent to the First Special District Court. However, the victims could not all attend, and the court ordered them to be remanded in custody. Yesterday, Judge Xiang Yinghua went to the Third Criminal Court to interrogate them. The Municipal Council's lawyer, Wang Yaotang, said that only five pawnshops had sent representatives to the court, and the rest were of the same nature, so they were not fully prosecuted. The witnesses stated the process of the two defendants switching the white silk. Zhou Xingshun and Li Aqing's confessions were cunning, and they hired lawyers to defend them. Judge Xiang ordered them to be remanded in custody pending sentencing.

Autopsy of Unnamed Man Who Fell to His Death Watching a Free Show

At 10:45 PM the night before last, a man of about seventeen or eighteen years old, wearing a white cloth short shirt and gray shorts, climbed onto the glass ceiling of the roof of a certain stage on Yunnan Road, Fuzhou Road, while the Four Volumes of Ji Gong's Biography and the Treasure Theft in the Xiangfu were being performed. He was watching a free show. Unexpectedly, the glass broke under the weight, causing the man to fall onto the stage. He was severely injured at the time. After reporting to the Laoku Police Station, an ambulance was summoned and he was taken to the Second Hospital for treatment. He died shortly after treatment was ineffective. Detective Xue Youwen was dispatched to investigate, but he could not find his family. Therefore, it is still unknown who he is. The body was carried to the Feilun Road Autopsy Room. Yesterday morning, the First Special District Court commissioned Prosecutor Tang and others to examine the body. According to Chinese Police Chief Zhang Wenjun's report of the previous situation, Mr. Tang ordered that the deceased, an unnamed man, had fallen to his death. Since no family was found, the body was handed over to the Pushan Villa for burial.

Sixty-Year-Old Woman Commits Suicide Out of Disgust for Life

Liang Huang, an old woman from Shaoxing, is 62 years old and lives with her daughter, Fu Liang, 40 years old, at No. 42 Laiyi Wharf Outside Street in the South City. The relationship between the mother and daughter is considered harmonious. At about 7:00 AM the day before yesterday, the woman took cold porridge to fill her hunger. Her daughter saw this and advised her mother not to eat cold food and to take cake from the room to fill her hunger. Unexpectedly, the old woman, for some unknown reason, suddenly had the idea of ending her life and secretly swallowed opium. At 3:00 PM, she began to groan in bed. Her daughter heard the sound and rushed over. Seeing her mother's pale face and rapid breathing, she knew that she had taken poison. She immediately hired a car to take her to Shanghai Hospital for treatment. However, the woman was old and weak, and had taken too much poison, so she could not be saved. She died at 2:45 AM yesterday morning.

Bank Inspection Report Compilation

Central Bank, Issuance Reserve 135th Inspection Report: According to Article 15 of the Central Bank Act, this council is responsible for inspecting the reserve fund for banknotes issued by this bank. The 235th inspection was held at the Issuance Bureau of this bank on June 10, 1935. The inspection results are hereby announced as follows: (A) Total amount of silver dollar banknotes issued: 97,618,784 silver dollars, including: 90,749,041 silver dollar banknotes and 6,873,742 subsidiary currency banknotes. Total amount of exchange note reserve: 97,608,784 silver dollars, including: 76,508,784 silver dollars in cash reserve. This cash reserve includes 72,377,975 silver dollars stored in the bank's issuing vault, 2,346,987 silver dollars stored in branches in ports, 1,794,222 silver dollars stored in industry, and guaranteed reserve equivalent to 11,100,000 Taiwan silver dollars. (B) Total amount of Customs Gold Unit (CGU) exchange notes issued: 372,224.7 CGU. Total amount of CGU exchange note reserve: 373,324.7 CGU. This reserve includes 7,350.95 taels of silver, converted to 373,314.7 CGU based on a fixed price of 0.50779. According to Article [blank] of the Central Bank Exchange Note Regulations, the cash reserve is 60% and the guaranteed reserve is 40%. The inspection results show that the cash exceeds the 60% requirement, and the guarantee is less than the 40% requirement, which is in accordance with the regulations. This report is hereby made. June 11, 1935. Chairman of the Supervisory Committee of the Central Bank, Li Fusun. Supervisors: Xie Mingxun, Bei Songsun, [blank] Runqing, Yu Qiaqing, Lin Kanghou, Xu Qing.

Four Banks, previous Issuance Reserve Report: The Four Banks Reserve Treasury is jointly established by the Central Bank, Jincheng, Yanye, China & South, and Continental Banks, and is dedicated to issuing banknotes for the China & South Bank. According to the treasury's issuance charter, the issuance of banknotes is fully reserved, with a cash reserve of at least 60% and a guaranteed reserve of at least 40%. It is announced once a week and verified by the auditors and accountants of the four banks. The 284th announcement of the Shanghai Reserve Treasury on June 8, 1935, is recorded below: Amount of banknotes in circulation: 13,317,5673 yuan, including: 8,920,0773 yuan in cash reserve and 4,573,900 yuan in guaranteed reserve.

Opening Ceremony of the Jingjiang Native Place Association Literacy School

The Jingjiang Shanghai Native Place Association, upon receiving joint instructions from the Municipal Party Department and the Social Bureau to establish a literacy school, immediately prepared actively in accordance. A literacy school was established within the Shanghai Jingjiang Elementary School in Ping An Li, Zhejiang Road, Simalu. The duration of study for students is set at one month per term, with daily class time from 7:00 PM to 5:00 PM. Teachers Hua Yizhi, Lin Fei, Yang Chunjiang, and Miao Jinrong of the Shanghai Jingjiang Elementary School were hired as professors. Enrollment began on the 1st of this month, and the response was very enthusiastic. As of the 9th, a total of 114 men and women had registered, and those continuing to register were still coming in an endless stream. Due to limited space, they could not be accommodated as much as desired. The opening ceremony was held yesterday at 7:00 PM, with 106 students in attendance. Wu Di-jun, a representative from the Municipal Party Department, was sent to the school for guidance. Mr. Hua Yizhi presided over the meeting, and the ceremony was conducted according to etiquette. The chairman reported the purpose of the meeting, followed by an address by Representative Wu, and speeches by the teachers. Stationery and books were then distributed, and the meeting adjourned around 9:00 PM.

Twelfth District Municipal United Association Rent Reduction Movement - Sends Personnel to Investigate the Situation to Achieve Results

The Tenth District Branch of the Shanghai First Special District Citizens' United Association, due to the closure of shops in the area, the economic depression, and the public's fear, and having received numerous letters from members requesting rent reduction, decided by the Executive Committee to carry out a rent reduction movement, starting with an investigation to provide factual proof. Personnel have now been dispatched to investigate and report on the situation. The association's jurisdiction includes housing in the Dagu Road Xinma Anli area. They requested that landlord Dehe Foreign Firm's Mr. Ma Lishi reduce rent. The association decided to provide assistance to achieve practical results. Additionally, Aiduya Road member Aidu Pharmacy and others requested that landlord Hengye Real Estate Company reduce rent. The association has already sent a letter requesting negotiation.

Post Office Mail Carrier An Weizun Missing - Please Pay Attention

An Weizun, a mail carrier at the Export Department of the local Postal Administration, is 40 years old, originally from Jiaozhou, Shandong, and currently resides at No. 231 Gongxing Road, Zhabei, Shanghai. He is usually loyal, honest, and sincere, and has no bad habits. However, at 5:00 PM on the 7th of this month, he suddenly went missing after leaving the office upon completing his duties. Several days have passed, and there is still no news. The mail carrier speaks with a Shandong accent. He was wearing a gray short shirt and pants when he went missing. Anyone with information about his whereabouts, please inform or accompany him to the Shanghai Postal Workers' Union at No. 5, Lane 538, Laobazi Road. This kindness will be greatly appreciated, and the union will provide a reward.

Paris Theater Showing Soviet Russian Song and Dance Film

The Paris Theater on Avenue Joffre is known for showing famous Soviet Russian films. The most valuable Soviet Russian films are often premiered at this theater. The Soviet Russian films that we have seen so far describe social anecdotes and the history of work struggles. Song and dance films have never been seen before. This time, the theater suddenly transported a Soviet Russian song and dance film. However, its style is definitely not like Hollywood's song and dance films that attract people with legs. It also has a profound meaning, implementing that music is the highest quality in art and can move sentient beings. The film tells the story of a flute player who brings many livestock to a grand banquet because of his flute playing. Beasts and humans get along in the same hall, devouring at will. A group of top-hatted gentlemen are all frightened and retreat. In fact, the gentlemen's level of musical appreciation is not even as good as that of the animals. The satire is profound, and the interest is deep. It is definitely not comparable to ordinary song and dance films. It is heard that this film will be publicly screened at the theater starting tomorrow.

Guanshengyuan Yumei New Decoration - Guanshengyuan Food Company, famous for manufacturing preserved tangerine peel, has recently launched Yumei, which has the same effect but different flavors. Although the taste is different from preserved tangerine peel, its nature is the same, with the effect of promoting salivation, quenching thirst, aiding digestion, and resolving phlegm. The raw materials are produced in the region, and the fruit embryos are large, crystal clear, and lovely. The intention of making Yumei is to symbolize its preciousness like jade among plums. The previous decoration was a long-style art box, priced at one dime per box. Now, in order to make it easier for buyers to carry, the company has specially made a large box and painted the scenery of Chaoshan on its surface. Six small boxes are packed into one large box, priced at six dimes per box. It is heard that since the redesign, buyers have been very enthusiastic.

Spring and Autumn

Tidbits

— (Microorganism)

The clamor for gender equality is deafening, but in trams and buses, we always only see "men giving way to women" seats, but never "women giving way to men" seats. Is this also considered gender equality!

Soft straw can bind hard tree firewood, which is called "soft firewood binding hard firewood" - the soft eats the hard. How is it different in the world when people deal with each other? When people glare and shout and let off a "big firecracker," I gently pour a ladle of "cold water" on it. The fuse is damp, and I guarantee it won't explode.

Urbanites enjoy all the other blessings; in the summer, they use electric fans and cool radiators; in the winter, they use electric heaters and warm radiators, but the "blessing of eating" and the "blessing of sleeping" cannot be compared to us country folks. Fresh and lively "fish and shrimp" are bought from the boat lady's hand as soon as they are caught, and fried in a hot pot. As soon as the sun goes down, after eating dinner, we undress and "fall asleep," and search in our dreams.

Yang Jiaoshan Was a Musician

— Chen Tuigan

Everyone who reads history knows that Mr. Yang Jiaoshan (Jisheng) of the Ming Dynasty was impeached for advising against opening the horse market. Later, he was promoted to Deputy Director of the Military Selection Department of the Ministry of War. He was killed for accusing Yan Song. Commentators say that the gentleman devoted his life to economics, but they did not know that he was also a musician. The other day, I saw Mr. Li Zhuowu's Chronicle of Yang Jiaoshan at a friend's house, which roughly said: When the gentleman was 34 years old and served as the Director of the Ministry of Personnel in Nanjing, he once studied rhythm and pitch with Han Gong Bangqi, Minister of War, and mastered its numbers in three months. Jiaoshan believed that music was not comparable to other studies. One cannot just talk about it; one must be able to make instruments and music oneself, and broadcast it in sound. Only when all are in harmony can one be called a musician. Therefore, he purchased knives, drills, axes, saws, tung wood, bamboo, silk, and lacquer. He first tried to make pipes, and then made zithers, harps, sheng, xiao, xun, chi, and the like. When he tried them, the sounds were all harmonious. When he combined all the instruments to play together, they were as consistent as one and all harmonious. Later, Han Gong ordered Jiaoshan to try to make twelve pipes of temperament, each with five notes and seven tones to form a tune. Jiaoshan exhausted his thoughts and neglected sleep and food for three days, and suddenly realized something. He finally made twelve pipes and presented them to Han Gong. From this, it is known that the name of music has spread throughout Nanjing. According to my research, Jiaoshan's reputation for being proficient in music was overshadowed by his integrity and loyalty, which led to its lack of transmission. It is truly regrettable. In recent years, Chinese people have been competing to study Western music, and no one has been able to improve the original Chinese music. If the method of making the twelve pipes musical instruments by Jiaoshan can be passed down, then there will also be a [blank] splendor in the aspect of national music.

Salesmen on the Tram

— Lan Shan

Recently, on trams on various routes, there is often a person carrying a small leather suitcase. He does not occupy a seat, but just stands in the middle. After saying "Ladies and gentlemen," he starts reciting. He speaks very quickly, as if he is singing a flowing opera. Whether he sells raisins, sweets, toothbrushes, peppermint lozenges, or Min Tan, the style of their speeches is mostly the same. He says that he is doing advertisements on the tram, and the price is particularly low; major companies such as Lao Da Fang and Tianlu Pharmacy also sell them, but the price is not as cheap as his. Then he takes out some samples from his leather suitcase for everyone to try. Sometimes it is two raisins, rolled in a thin piece of paper, and each person is given a share. Some people take it and eat it politely; some people take it in their hands embarrassedly. But no one is willing to spend two dimes to buy five packs of his. So the frustrated salesman gets off the bus.

Yesterday I wanted to go to Carter Road. During the long tram journey, several salesmen came one after another. One was selling Min Tan. After his speech, every passenger had a Min Tan in their mouth. Perhaps it was because of the hot weather and dry mouth, everyone welcomed the Min Tan and made a few dimes in transactions. A little later, another person came to sell peppermint lozenges. As usual, after finishing his speech, he lightly rubbed the peppermint on each guest's temples and under the nostrils to test its effectiveness. He was very fair, and even the modern lady sitting diagonally across from me was rubbed twice. When all the passengers' eyes were focused on her face, she turned red with embarrassment. In order to cover up her shame, she simply dug out two dimes from her silver clip and bought a lozenge. Sure enough, the atmosphere eased as a result.

Although salesmen on the tram is a clever form of business, I always think that it hinders the order on the tram a bit.

Miss Guo

— Xiaodong

When Miss Guo was seventeen, she was still a naive girl in Town S. After living in Port S with her mother for five years, she actually turned into a city lady. Her fluffy hair was tied with a black satin floral hoop; long eyelashes were under her slender painted eyebrows, and her cherry lips were slightly lipsticked. Although her face was not powdered, she already felt very charming and moving! The new fashions of the era changed several times a day, making the young men of Town S madly infatuated!

According to Mr. Chun's comments, Miss Guo's face is not very beautiful, but her clothes are very alluring. Her figure is somewhat like the movie star Greta Garbo, and she speaks fluent Shanghai dialect. Such a woman was seen for the first time ever in Town S. Mr. Chun often said to his friends: "I've seen thousands of scorpions, but I've never seen such a lovely girl. My eyes are dazzled and it's hard to speak, and my soul has flown away for half a day." She has such intoxicating magic, no wonder she has caused a sensation in the entire Town S.

What Miss Guo did in Port S is quite suspicious to idle people. Most people speculate and explore, and are sure that she is a dancer, because she speaks very fluently about dancing. However, Miss Guo has a strange temper and is unwilling to entertain people when she sees them. This is the factor that brought her trouble, so she cannot be allowed to stay in Town S. But if she is not a business person, why bother to entertain these mad bees and butterflies? Although she left Town S, her reputation is kept clear, but there are many people who miss her after she left.

Acknowledgment - The Southeast Pagoda Shadows book, edited and printed by the Beijing-Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Bureau, has now been published. It includes thirty-four famous giant pagodas along the railway line. In addition to finely printed photos of each pagoda, it also provides a brief description of its origin and scenery. The actual price per book is two dimes. It is sold at major stations, business offices, and railway hotels along the railway line. Thank you for the gift of two copies.

Social Photo

A Strange Man in the Plague Hospital

— Yi Sheng

In early summer, the hottest day of the year arrived. Di, feeling the threat of the scorching heat, quickly recalled an experience I personally had last summer, worth recording. A little after three o'clock before dawn, a burst of stomach pain woke me up. The pain was followed by diarrhea, which got increasingly worse. I decided to go to the plague hospital. I asked about the nearest one, but the alarming consultation fee forced me to endure until after seven o'clock before going. After the examination, they said I needed to be hospitalized. My family helped me upstairs. The floor was divided into two rows of wards, with a corridor in the middle. I entered a second-class ward in the first room on the north side, and, exhausted, fell asleep.

"... Gao Ma, ah... buy him ice cream, ah... let him eat it, ah, it's so hot, ah... Gao Ma, ah, fix it, ah..."

This unexpected, drawn-out, upside-down kind of shouting startled me awake. It was ceaseless. After a while, the Yangzhou accent revealed that the only maid was yelling and promising from afar, trying to stop him from making noise. It was quiet for a while, but soon he started with new tricks:

"Sell tofu pudding, ah... let him eat it, ah... go buy it, ah, Gao Ma, ah..."

The impatient scolding was also in Yangzhou dialect and could silence the noise for five minutes. Afterward, the "old noise returned," but the object of the call, Gao Ma, was changed to Miss Wang. The pleading voice continued persistently, as if it would not stop until it achieved its goal. The accommodating, sometimes scolding, sometimes coaxing tone told everyone that Miss Wang was the nurse, and she was responsible for taking care of this gentleman.

After my accompanying family member investigated, they reported to me like telling a story, breaking the mystery of this period, although it still didn't solve the annoyance of continuing to hear the strange shouts.

In the last first-class room in the south row, lived a middle-aged man. This man had a long beard, messy hair, a thin, pale face, bare feet in leather slippers, and was still wearing a cotton-padded jacket and pants. He paced back and forth in the room. If he saw someone peeking, he would know to stop shouting temporarily. After people watched for a long time, they didn't want to avoid him anymore.

According to the hospital servant, Gao Ma, "This man's family was originally quite well-off, and he had talent. While living here, besides eating and drinking, he would occasionally recite lines from books or say a few words in a foreign language. It was only because he was doing business on the stock exchange that he made a lot of money. Last year, one night, one of his young, playful disciples started teasing the master, pretending to be serious and scaring him, saying, 'The market has changed a lot today, and your business will lose to a certain extent!' He was immediately frightened and went crazy. Although they tried to explain it in every way and prove the truth, nothing worked! The hospital director is related to him and let him stay in the hospital for treatment. He came here after the plague hospital opened last year and has been here ever since. We have suffered enough from him! His family, even his wife, are so annoyed by his nonsense that they have lost heart and are not happy to visit him, but they leave some money for him to use, to support him in his old age!"

Although I didn't have the ability to watch this farce continue and couldn't stand the afternoon sun shining through the north window, which might cause a plague, I requested to be discharged from the hospital that day. I didn't object to this half-crazy, half-awake strange man continuing to live there, eating some seasonal foods, or even some strange things he thought of, as long as all the other plague patients on the floor, out of respect for the hospital director or out of sympathy and pity, no one would take the lead in starting trouble.

Besides, this man went crazy because of the high heat of the stock exchange. If he wasn't allowed to live in the plague hospital, where else could he live? His relative's decision to let him stay was indeed very appropriate. He is truly a wonderful person!

I don't know if this man is still in this plague hospital this year. I miss this poor, strange man!

A Record of Incense Drifting from the Imperial Boat

— Originally written by Princess Der Ling of Qing Dynasty, translated by Qin Shouou

Its top was also exquisitely carved and lacquered with a row of glazed tiles using the best wood. From a distance, it looked no different from the real thing, which shows the exquisite construction! The Empress Dowager herself sat on this imperial boat, and four of us eight female officials—I was one of them—were selected to accompany her on the boat. This could be considered a fully aristocratic suburban banquet.

Once the Empress Dowager decided, everyone in the palace immediately busied themselves with preparations. First, everyone gathered around her at the dock where the imperial boat was moored, watching the little eunuchs in charge of rowing the boat tidy up the oars and stand in their designated positions. Then, we four female officials carefully helped the Empress Dowager onto the boat, allowing the old woman to sit comfortably on her specially prepared throne. Next, someone opened the two tall, large dock doors, letting the imperial boat slowly and steadily float out. The eunuchs who rowed the boat were well-trained and could minimize the swaying common when rowing a boat.

After leaving the dock, there was a short tributary. After about four or five minutes, the imperial boat appeared on the mirror-like surface of Kunming Lake. The smile on the corner of the Empress Dowager's mouth, although still a smile, never disappeared. She was even happier to see the vivid lake scenery in front of her, and her eyes were filled with vibrant light. The red sun in the sky turned the lake water into a golden liquid, making her feel happy. And we all felt happy because of her happiness. (337)

Crying for Xie Da's Visit to the Temple

— Zheng Manqing

Sadly chanting, crying for Xie Da: soaking with tears, bitterly recalling the day of his death, shaking hands without a sound. Unable to bear to sit and look, unable to leave the door. Wanting to speak but sobbing again, his younger brother is there to greet me (referring to Zhiliu). Zhiliu's children stand full of the steps, how can they know the pain of what has happened? Parting in life is also a death, so desolate, like separated by generations. Returning, unable to sleep, before dawn the crows are already crowing. Sure enough, news of his death has arrived, old friends are all shocked. I doubt this, can you be reborn after death? Entrusting twin carps to summon your soul, passing words to the nine netherworlds. Only you cannot die, the mountain is not yet formed. In the hall, the white-haired mourn, throughout the land, relatives and friends cry. Soul, why don't you return, soul, how unsacred. Those who have long passed away, a sorrowful city on the land. On your birthday, you were often sick, your writing surpassing Chang Qing. Now you know nothing, people sigh that a great beam has collapsed. Having known each other for a lifetime, loving each other like brothers. The birds sing sadly in spring, who will listen to their warbling again?

Little Western Paradise

— Written by Zhang Henshui

Chapter 14: Gaining Insight, Westerners Should Build Without Regrets, Ten Kinds of Lovesickness

Zhiqian smiled and said, "It's not just that, I think Beihai has really fallen in love with this girl, he can't help himself. Now this girl is worried about finding a grain store because she can't solve the problem of food for her family of three. If Beihai wants to talk to her about love, he must first take care of the meals for these three people. He is still worried about not being able to fill his own stomach, how can he support two generations? Therefore, I upheld this great and impartial heart and advised her in front of the girl, hoping they would not get close." You Rong sighed and smiled: "You are wrong. People who should fall in love talk about going through fire and water without hesitation. How can lack of food be an obstacle? If this girl is willing to marry Wang Jun, they can be a poor couple. Speaking of Wang Jun, he will eventually get married. Adding a woman should not be talked about as a burden. Now it's just the girl's grandmother and mother, who are considered extra people. But Wang Jun's family are farmers. Since they can send their son out to go to school, the grain is probably enough to eat. Adding two people to eat may not be a big problem. Why don't you wait for Wang Jun to come and ask him carefully? If he really doesn't have the ability, it's not too late to dissuade him. Otherwise, facilitating other people's marriage is ten times more meritorious than saving a life. If they have no money for the wedding, to be honest, I can help with twenty or fifty dollars." Saying that, her face was full of smiles, showing a happy look. Zhiqian hesitated and stood up, looking at him. (237)

Ministry of Education's Zhong Daozan Inspects Qingdao's Vocational Education Report

Qingdao's vocational education has a short history, starting in 1934. The private Lixian Middle School used to run several civil engineering classes, but they were suspended for a few years. Currently, the city has a senior vocational class in the municipal middle school, a junior general vocational class, a junior agriculture class at the municipal Licun Normal School, a senior civil engineering class at the private Lixian Middle School, and a junior business class at the private Chongde Middle School, totaling three senior classes and three junior classes, with a total of 224 students and expenses of 32,575 yuan. However, at the beginning of operation, the facilities are mostly simple, and the results have not yet been shown. Efforts are needed to enrich and establish a good foundation. However, the city's primary and secondary schools are able to pay attention to labor education, and the factory labor literacy education is well-managed. The points to be noted for the city's vocational education, labor education, and labor education are divided as follows: 1. Considering the current situation in the city, attention should be paid to: (1) Cooperation between the mechanical engineering department and the naval factory and Shandong University's School of Engineering, (2) Civil engineering and construction department, (3) Horticulture department focusing on the improvement of fruit trees and vegetables, and cooperation with the city's agricultural and forestry office and Shandong University's School of Agriculture, (4) Business department, (5) Home economics department can be attached to the Sacred Heart Girls' Middle School or the Municipal Girls' Middle School. When each department has achieved success, then plan to establish chemical technology and other departments. 2. Vocational students in the city value further education. Therefore, school facilities and teaching content still focus on preparing for further education. The problem of vocational training itself is neglected. It is urgent to improve teaching methods to correct their wrong ideas.

3. The senior and junior vocational classes of the municipal middle school lack equipment, and the curriculum is too complex. For example, the electrical engineering of the senior applied chemistry department, the electrical common sense, mechanical common sense, simple chemistry, and commercial common sense of the junior vocational department. Since the goals are not clear, learning cannot be specialized. The senior applied chemistry department only manufactures a few bars of soap in the whole year. The metal tools made by the junior department are not precise. The practice hours are few, and the content is not rich enough. It is urgent to improve.

Because the senior applied chemistry department of the school has no equipment, it is not as well-equipped as the mechanical department. It is planned to change to running a mechanical department. If it is implemented, the summer vacation of the second and third academic years should be fully utilized, and the duration should be extended appropriately to make up for the lack of technology in the first academic year. Even if it is not changed, it should be done in the same way to help.

4. The practice of the junior agricultural department of the municipal Licun Middle School uses the farm equipment of the city's agricultural and forestry office. All guidance work is done by the staff of the office, which is convenient and effective. However, there are only eight hours of practice per week, while electric training and martial arts have five hours per week. It should be improved.

The office plans to open another farm for students to practice. The principle of economic production should be adopted. The original farm of the office should still be used for experimental work. Third-year students should also be required to serve as interns in the office to improve their research skills.

5. The commercial subjects in the ordinary business department of the private Chongde Junior High School are very few. The amount of Chinese, English, Mathematics, Natural Science, History, Geography, etc. is almost the same as that of junior high school. The practice equipment only has two typewriters and a simple school store. The timetable should be rearranged to make the purpose simple and train small-scale store managers and large store clerks. 6. The curriculum of the civil engineering department of the private Lixian Middle School includes metalworking and mechanical practice and woodworking practice for two hours each. Considering the content, it has little to do with civil engineering. Woodworking practice should pay attention to house structure models. The existing tenon practice is not accurate. Architectural drawing is only two hours per week, architectural practice is only four hours, and German, Chinese, Mathematics, Physics, and Chemistry are all more than six hours per week. The equipment is also too simple. All should be improved.

7. The home economics equipment of the private Sacred Heart Girls' Middle School is perfect, and the sewing, weaving, embroidery, and jacquard results are excellent. Attention is paid to art. It should be ordered to set up a home economics department immediately.

8. The labor education equipment of primary and secondary schools in the city has a foundation. In the future, boys should focus on metal and woodworking, pay attention to the infusion of scientific knowledge, girls should focus on housework, pay attention to the improvement of family affairs. At the same time, labor teachers should also be trained in summer labor courses.

9. The labor literacy education of the Huaxin Yarn Factory is divided into four stages: (1) Literacy education for six months, (2) Civic education for six months, (3) Junior vocational tutoring for one year, (4) Senior vocational tutoring for four years. The first three are the education that ordinary workers should study, and the latter is free to choose to study. There are only more than 300 of the factory's 1,700 workers who have not received the above training. However, two classes are held every morning and evening, each lasting 80 minutes, all after work. The general workers are inevitably tired and cannot get full benefits. It can be changed to attending classes before working. Since the class time is short, it will not hinder the work, and the spirit is refreshed, and the education will be more effective. It should be consulted to the Social Affairs Bureau for consideration.

The City's Higher and General Examination Schedule Has Been Completed

Five Days from the 17th to the 21st of This Month

This Year's Middle School Scholarship Exam Sponsored by the Ding Bureau

Scheduled to be Held on the 24th of This Month. Quota: 12. Register as soon as possible

The Public Works Department has specially set up twelve middle school scholarships to reward students with good character and learning and with poor families to go to school. The details have been reported in the previous reports. It is learned that this year's middle school scholarship examination will be held on the 24th of this month. The method is as follows:

Scholarship Method: The quota for this scholarship is twelve, including scholarships for students entering from schools established by the Public Works Department, four for boys and two for girls, and scholarships for students entering from schools not established by the Public Works Department, four for boys and two for girls. After receiving this scholarship, all tuition fees are waived, and the school provides books and stationery free of charge. The period is three years, and there are inspections at the end of the first and second years to determine whether to stay or leave based on the grades. Those with excellent grades can continue to read all three years of junior high school for free.

Scheduled Examination: The qualifications for this scholarship include not only excellent academic performance, but also whether the family is really poor. A written test will be held on Chinese, history, geography, natural science, English, and mathematics. Candidates must have completed elementary school and be no more than thirteen years old. In addition, the parents of the candidates must be residents of the Public Concession. The examination date has been set for June 24th. Those who wish to take the exam must first fill out an application form at their alma mater and then have the principal of the alma mater register on behalf of the applicant to the Public Works Department before the 20th of this month.

Public Health Research Association: A Competition for Essays on Bedbug Research Initiated for the People

The Public Health Research Association, for the sake of the citizens, was organized by Liu Liangmo, Ma Zongdang, Peng Sanmei, and others. Mr. Liu and the others are all employed in social service organizations such as the YMCA and YWCA, and have deep contact with the public on a daily basis. They deeply understand the suffering of ordinary people from bedbugs, but social figures do not pay attention to this problem. Therefore, they initiated a campaign this spring to eliminate bedbugs, in order to seek the welfare of the common people. Now, in order to arouse the attention of biologists nationwide to bedbugs, they have launched an essay competition on bedbug life research, and printed and distributed the competition rules to universities across the country, so that students studying biology in various schools can specialize in research during the summer vacation.

Huxi Weiming Basketball Team Wins Championship

Fufeng Loses 43 to 27, Placing Second

The final match of the 2nd Huxi Basketball Tournament between Weiming and Fufeng was held at 5 p.m. yesterday. After forty minutes of fierce battle, Weiming defeated Fufeng 43 to 27 and won the championship. In the first half, Weiming led 23 to 14. Referees Zhang Wenyuan and Shi Zhaokang immediately invited Mr. Zhou Jiaqi to present the awards after the game. Here is a brief description of the battle. Before 5 p.m., fans had already sat around the basketball court, quietly waiting for the two teams to start the game. The enthusiasm was unprecedented. As soon as 5 p.m. arrived, the referee blew the whistle to announce the start of the battle. Fufeng took the lead and immediately took a five-point lead with penalties and throws. Weiming, seeing that the situation was not good, requested a timeout. The Fufeng ball was smooth, and forward Fang Shouxiang fought alone, throwing and hitting continuously, occupying an absolute advantage of twelve to west. But after entering, Weiming cheered up unusually, catching up step by step, fighting tighter and tighter, and the scores were getting closer and closer. Until twelve to thirteen, Fufeng collapsed and was overtaken by Weiming with twenty-three to fourteen, taking the lead in the first half. Fufeng worked hard to counterattack in the afternoon, but it was beyond its ability and ran into walls everywhere. Therefore, it was eventually overtaken by Weiming all the way and did not get a chance to overtake. Looking at the skills of both sides, there are merits. Weiming's throwing skills are indeed superior, so it can win the final victory, and the defensive skills are also very impressive, but there are too many fouls, which is a deficiency. If Fufeng had scored more points in the foul penalty, the number of wins and losses would still be unknown. It turned out that Fufeng had once defeated Weiming 30 to 22 once. Now, Fufeng had 23 free throw opportunities, but only hit six times. The difference between one gain and one loss is not small. This is a major reason for Fufeng's loss. In addition, forward general Zhai Songtao was unable to participate due to illness, which was also a fatal blow to the entire team of Zaofeng. In terms of talent, Chen Tianguo, Hu Yepei, and Liang Dusheng of Weiming are all outstanding talents. Fang Shouyi, Gu Chongshan, and Sun Yiqin of Fufeng also had many good performances. It is not easy for the business community to achieve this result in amateur sports. The annual Huxi Cup basketball game ended in cheers. Here are the scores of both sides:

Finance Spot Trends Very Active Gold Standard Falls Then Suddenly Rises in Reaction

——Result, Agreement Two Yuan Three Jiao——

The gold market initially followed the rise and fall of the overseas silver market yesterday. Unexpectedly, spot sales were brisk, and adding water caused it to rise to around 30 yuan. Short-term futures presented a heavy threat to short sellers, stimulating buying and causing a rebound. The future market became uncertain. Early morning overseas calls indicated that in two days, London was even and the US rose. The forward silver price in Montreaux also rose by more than one point. Exchange rates all contracted, and London raw gold rose half a penny. People's hearts were weary, as the voices of US silver party members urging the government to make money were again high. Off-site ready transactions were sold, retreating to 6134 yuan. Buyers took advantage of the low price and were pulled up. The Central Bank's listed prices were announced, with both the UK and the US rising. Customs gold units fell by one point, and the listed gold standard price fell to 846 yuan and eight jiao, with little impact. After opening, it was slightly stable. The exchange market was loose and excessive, fueling selling and causing a decline. However, because the Shanghai Bank worked hard to dig up spot forward orders, buyers saw low prices and acted, managing to maintain the level. The HSBC Bank's listed prices were announced, with the UK rising by 1.5 and the US rising by 2.5. The market was still in progress at this time. Later, it was heard that pure gold spot prices had actually risen by 25 yuan, and there were still many buyers, stimulating buying and causing a gradual rise. Sassoon reacted by bidding up the US dollar, and the exchange market trend broke through the 71 yuan mark. Banks took advantage of the high price to push out orders, and large accounts also had sales. Soon after, they took advantage of the situation to continue buying, gradually rising back to above 70 yuan. At noon, it was relatively stable. In the afternoon, the market was quiet, and the opening was late. After opening, buyers suddenly surged, immediately causing a price increase. Those supplying at high prices were quite strong, but because of the reported fall in Indian silver, An'na struggled more. The exchange market was normal and turned flat. Later, Indian silver fell another six An'na for the second time, and Sassoon and others continued to bid up, reporting another rise. Unexpectedly, large accounts successively unloaded their holdings, and the multi-party lineup showed signs of being unable to support the market. The market suddenly weakened at the close. The market situation for the day was weak and then firm, and it was still difficult to be certain about people's hearts. The market situation for the day will now be recorded:

Chunyuan, Yongchang, Dayifeng, Yongqian, Changxiang, Yongli, Dadecheng, Yuanchang, Yongfuxing, and Yongwanfeng all advanced and rose to 8 yuan and 2 jiao. Hengyu and Fuxingyong sold strips, retreating to 7 yuan. Banque de l'Indochine ate August US dollars at 875. As a result, the current month continued to be up 2 fen and 2.5 li, July was up 2 fen, August was up 1 fen and 7.5 li, September was up 1 fen and 2.5 li, October was up 1 fen and 2.5 li, and November was up 1 fen and 2.5 li.

Rice Arrivals are Scarcer and Prices Rise

Yesterday, the sources of rice from various states in South Shanghai were particularly scarce, with only 1,700 to 1,800 shi arriving (cargo No. 7-8). The sales floor was also dull, with only the Qingdao gang taking 300 bags. Prices increased, but market sentiment seemed unstable. Prices for various thick japonica and middle-market late rice increased by several fen or jiao. High-quality thin indica rice was expensive, and sales were relatively slow, with little activity. Supply and demand for varieties such as Yinbian Yuan and Dujian were similar, with no changes. Yesterday in North Shanghai, sixteen to seventeen cargo ships arrived from various routes along the river. Each cargo on the market sold, white japonica turned dull, thin indica was average, and the remaining cargoes continued to move. Market prices for white japonica slightly softened, thin indica stabilized, white yuan remained firm, and other varieties saw little change.

Foreign rice sales remained active. In addition to various gangs from inland Zhejiang Province continuing to ship goods, the Nanjing gang saw a sudden surge in sales. Gangs from Xunqing and Zhenjiang in the Yangtze River region also inquired. The market continued to expand. If sales continue to be strong today and tomorrow, prices may need to increase further. Yesterday, Saigon No. 1 and small-grain rice rose by 1 jiao, while No. 3 rice and broken rice remained relatively stable. A total of 15,000 bags of various Saigon rices, 7,000 bags of small-grain rice, over 2,000 bags of various Siam Gao Gong rices, and 500 bags of customer indica were sold throughout the day, distributed to Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Anhui, and the local street.

Soybean Cake Sales Active Due to Rain in the Countryside

Yesterday, the spot market for soybean cake saw increased activity, due to cloudy weather and the possibility of rain in the countryside, giving hope for rice transplanting and farming. As a result, prices rose by two to three fen in both the morning and afternoon. A total of 16,000 to 17,000 pieces of cake were traded (see the market price column for prices). Soybean sales were still not weak, with a total of eighteen to nineteen truckloads of beans sold across the market, but market conditions remained generally flat and tired, mainly due to pressure from Shandong soybeans (yesterday, it was heard that fifty truckloads of Sipingjie beans were traded at a price of only 3.5 yuan), so the market was unable to rally.

North and South Goods: New Bamboo Branches for Cocoons Urgently Need Improvement

The cocoon bamboo branches produced in Zhangzhou have good seedlings this year, and the estimated harvest is expected to be 60-70%. According to a letter, new products can be seen at the end of this month. Due to news of a poor harvest of Jinshan branches produced in Guangdong, merchants there have raised prices. However, given the current financial situation, sales may be difficult at that time. Moreover, the quality of the goods is inferior to Guangdong products, and improvement is essential. If the lychees are pointed, without flesh, and inedible, they are also useless and should be removed to stimulate sales. This year, as the Jinshan branches are in short supply, it is imperative to take the opportunity to improve the products in order to expand sales.

Silk and Tea: Silk Prices Differ by Only a Few Yuan

The day before yesterday was Easter, and Western merchants at home and abroad were closed for business, so the silk market was even more deserted. In recent days, many silk telegrams have been sent from Shanghai to foreign countries, but few have received responses. It is said that the difference in prices between the two sides is only about twenty yuan. However, due to extremely erratic exchange rates, it is difficult to conclude transactions. If gold prices can stabilize slightly, it should not be difficult to break the deadlock of protective mutual observation.

Zhenmei Green Tea Continues to Fall

Yesterday, the market for Zhuangzhenmei green tea was slightly dull. The prices of goods from Suian, Tunxi, Wenzhou, and other routes resumed their downward trend. The average price of pumped-core ordinary Zhenmei fell by three to four yuan compared to the previous day. The sales of green tea from Pingshui and Tuzhuang were even more sluggish. Six to seven-tenths of the raw tea from various counties in Zhejiang Province is still held by tea farmers, with no one buying it.
